### [30] [Nexus : An Agentic Framework for Time Series Forecasting](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14389v1)
*Sarkar Snigdha Sarathi Das,Palash Goyal,Mihir Parmar,Nanyun Peng,Vishy Tirumalashetty,Chun-Liang Li,Rui Zhang,Jinsung Yoon,Tomas Pfister*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent时间序列预测框架，架构可迁移。

TL;DR: Nexus通过多智能体分解预测阶段，有效结合数值与上下文推理，显著提升LLM在现实时间序列预测中的表现，匹配或超越专业模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有TSFMs忽视文本信号，而LLM零样本预测性能不稳定，需要弥合数值与上下文推理的差距。

Method: 提出Nexus多智能体框架，将预测分解为宏观/微观波动隔离、上下文整合、最终合成等专门阶段。

Result: 在Zillow和股票数据上，Nexus匹配或超越SOTA TSFMs和LLM基线，并产生高质量推理轨迹。

Conclusion: 现实预测是智能体推理问题，超越序列建模。

中文摘要：时间序列预测不仅仅是数值外推，而常常需要结合非结构化上下文数据（如新闻或事件）进行推理。专门的时间序列基础模型（TSFMs）擅长基于数值模式进行预测，但它们对现实世界的文本信号缺乏感知。相反，虽然大语言模型（LLMs）正作为零样本预测器出现，但其在不同领域和上下文基础中的表现仍参差不齐。为弥合这一差距，我们提出了Nexus，一个多智能体预测框架，将预测分解为专门阶段：隔离宏观和微观时间波动，并在获得上下文信息时将其整合，最终合成预测结果。这种分解使Nexus能够从季节性信号适应到波动性的、事件驱动的信息，而无需依赖外部统计锚点或单一提示。我们表明，当前一代的LLMs具有比先前认知更强的内在预测能力，这关键取决于数值和上下文推理的组织方式。在严格超出LLM知识截止日期后的数据（涵盖Zillow房地产指标和波动性的股票市场权益）上评估，Nexus始终匹配或超越最先进的TSFMs和强大的LLM基线。除了数值准确性，Nexus还产生高质量的推理轨迹，明确展示每个预测背后的基本驱动因素。我们的结果证实，现实世界预测是一个远远超出序列建模的智能体推理问题。

Original abstract: Time series forecasting is not just numerical extrapolation, but often requires reasoning with unstructured contextual data such as news or events. While specialized Time Series Foundation Models (TSFMs) excel at forecasting based on numerical patterns, they remain unaware to real-world textual signals. Conversely, while LLMs are emerging as zero-shot forecasters, their performance remains uneven across domains and contextual grounding. To bridge this gap, we introduce Nexus, a multi-agent forecasting framework that decomposes prediction into specialized stages: isolating macro-level and micro-level temporal fluctuations, and integrating contextual information when available before synthesizing a final forecast. This decomposition enables Nexus to adapt from seasonal signals to volatile, event-driven information without relying on external statistical anchors or monolithic prompting. We show that current-generation LLMs possess substantially stronger intrinsic forecasting ability than previously recognized, depending critically on how numerical and contextual reasoning are organized. Evaluated on data strictly succeeding LLM knowledge cutoffs spanning Zillow real estate metrics and volatile stock market equities, Nexus consistently matches or outperforms state-of-the-art TSFMs and strong LLM baselines. Beyond numerical accuracy, Nexus produces high-quality reasoning traces that explicitly show the fundamental drivers behind each forecast. Our results establish that real-world forecasting is an agentic reasoning problem extending well beyond only sequence modeling.

### [31] [Learning to Build the Environment: Self-Evolving Reasoning RL via Verifiable Environment Synthesis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14392v1)
*Yucheng Shi,Zhenwen Liang,Kishan Panaganti,Dian Yu,Wenhao Yu,Haitao Mi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 模型构建环境自演进，与代码优化agent的环境构建直接相关。

TL;DR: 提出基于环境构建与求解-验证不对称性的自我改进方法EvoEnv，在Qwen3-4B模型上获得3.3%的相对提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自我改进方法依赖数据生成，但易被模型欺骗；需要创建结构上难以被模型轻易解决的训练环境，以保持奖励信号的有效性。

Method: EvoEnv：单策略生成器-求解器方法，从种子合成Python环境，经过阶段验证、语义自审、难度校准和新颖性检查后用于强化学习训练。

Result: 在Qwen3-4B-Thinking上，EvoEnv将平均分从72.4提升至74.8（相对+3.3%），而固定环境方法导致性能下降。

Conclusion: 稳定自我改进的关键在于模型学习构建难度结构上超出自身能力的世界，而非依赖更多合成数据。

中文摘要：我们追求一种自我改进语言模型的愿景，其中模型不仅生成问题或轨迹进行模仿，而是构建训练它的环境。在零数据推理强化学习中，这将自我改进从数据生成循环重新框架为环境构建循环，其中每个工件都是可重用的可执行对象，用于采样实例、计算参考分数和评分响应。这一愿景能否持续改进取决于一个特性：环境必须表现出稳定的求解-验证不对称性，即模型必须能够编写一个它不能可靠地在自然语言中在新鲜实例上执行的神谕。这种不对称性有两种互补形式。某些任务在算法上难以推理但作为代码却微不足道：动态规划或图遍历，编译一次后，产生无限多个校准实例。其他任务本质上难以求解但易于验证，如植入的子集和或约束满足。两者都在提议和求解之间创造了一个持久的差距，政策无法通过欺骗验证器来弥合，正是这种差距使奖励在学习者改进时保持信息性。我们在EvoEnv中实例化这一观点，这是一种单一策略生成器、求解器方法，从十个种子合成Python环境，并在经过阶段验证、语义自我审查、求解器相对难度校准和新颖性检查后才接受它们。最强证据来自已经强大的领域：在Qwen3-4B-Thinking上，固定的公共数据RLVR和固定手工制作的环境RLVR降低了平均值，而EvoEnv将其从72.4提高到74.8，相对提升3.3%。我们认为，稳定的自我改进不依赖于产生更多的合成数据，而是依赖于学习构建世界，其难度在结构上保持超出自身能力范围。

Original abstract: We pursue a vision for self-improving language models in which the model does not merely generate problems or traces to imitate, but constructs the environments that train it. In zero-data reasoning RL, this reframes self-improvement from a data-generation loop into an environment-construction loop, where each artifact is a reusable executable object that samples instances, computes references, and scores responses. Whether this vision sustains improvement hinges on a single property: the environments must exhibit stable solve--verify asymmetry, the model must be able to write an oracle once that it cannot reliably execute in natural language on fresh instances. This asymmetry takes two complementary forms. Some tasks are algorithmically hard to reason through but trivial as code: a dynamic program or graph traversal, compiled once, yields unboundedly many calibrated instances. Others are intrinsically hard to solve but easy to verify, like planted subset-sum or constraint satisfaction. Both create a durable gap between proposing and solving that the policy cannot close by gaming the verifier, and it is this gap that keeps reward informative as the learner improves. We instantiate this view in EvoEnv, a single-policy generator, solver method that synthesizes Python environments from ten seeds and admits them only after staged validation, semantic self-review, solver-relative difficulty calibration, and novelty checks. The strongest evidence comes from the already-strong regime: on Qwen3-4B-Thinking, fixed public-data RLVR and fixed hand-crafted environment RLVR reduce the average, while EvoEnv improves it from 72.4 to 74.8, a relative gain of 3.3%. Stable self-improvement, we suggest, depends not on producing more synthetic data, but on models learning to construct worlds whose difficulty stays structurally beyond their own reach.

</details>

*Hongyu Wang,Jingquan Wang,Bocheng Zou,Radu Serban,Dan Negrut*

  <summary>Details</summary>

中文摘要：世界模型已成为构建交互式模拟环境的强大范式，近期的基于视频的方法在生成视觉上合理的动力学方面展示了令人印象深刻的进展。然而，由于这些模型通常从视频中推断动力学并将其表示为潜在状态，它们并未明确强制执行物理约束。因此，生成的视频推演在物理上不合理，表现出不稳定的接触、扭曲形状或不一致的运动。在本文中，我们提出了一个通过可执行模拟代码构建基于物理的世界模型的智能体框架。该框架协调了规划、代码生成、视觉审查和物理分析智能体。规划智能体将自然语言提示转换为结构化的场景规划，代码智能体将其实现为可执行的模拟代码，视觉审查智能体提供视觉反馈，而物理分析智能体检查物理一致性。基于反馈迭代地修订代码，直到模拟与提示要求和物理约束相匹配。实验结果表明，我们的框架在物理准确性、指令保真度和视觉质量方面优于先进的基于视频的模型，并可用于多种场景，包括驾驶模拟和具身机器人任务。

Original abstract: World models have emerged as a powerful paradigm for building interactive simulation environments, with recent video-based approaches demonstrating impressive progress in generating visually plausible dynamics. However, because these models typically infer dynamics from video and represent them in latent states, they do not explicitly enforce physical constraints. As a result, the generated video rollouts are not physically plausible, exhibiting unstable contacts, distorted shapes, or inconsistent motion. In this paper, we present an agentic framework constructing physics-based world models through executable simulation code. The framework coordinates planning, code generation, visual review, and physics analysis agents. The planning agent converts the natural language prompt into a structured scene plan, the code agent implements it as executable simulation code, and the visual review agent provide visual feedback while the physics analysis agent checks physical consistency. The code is iteratively revised based on the feedback until the simulation matches the prompt reqirements and physical constraints. Experimental results show that our framework outperforms advanced video-based models in physical accuracy, instruction fidelity and visual quality, which could be applied to various scenarios including driving simulation and embodied robot tasks.

### [33] [Synthesizing POMDP Policies: Sampling Meets Model-checking via Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14440v1)
*Debraj Chakraborty,Anirban Majumdar,Prince Mathew,Sayan Mukherjee,Jean-François Raskin*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 整合采样与模型检查的POMDP策略合成，对agent规划方法有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 提出一种集成抽样、自动机学习和模型检测的POMDP综合框架，能在正则策略假设下提供形式化保证，实验证明可解决现有工具难以处理的阈值安全问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于抽样的方法虽可扩展但缺乏形式化保证，而形式化综合技术虽提供正确性保证但可扩展性差且一般不可判定。需要一种既能保证正确性又具有实用可扩展性的方法。

Method: 受Angluin L*算法启发，使用抽样作为成员查询预言，模型检测作为等价查询预言，交替进行策略学习和验证，综合出有限状态控制器，并证明在策略为正则时相对完备。

Result: 原型实现成功解决了阈值安全问题的实例，这些实例对现有形式化综合工具具有挑战性，表明方法有效。

Conclusion: 该算法可作为组合方法中的有价值组件，有助于处理POMDP综合问题的固有难度。

中文摘要：部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP）是不确定性下决策的标准框架。基于抽样的方法具有良好的可扩展性，但缺乏形式化正确性保证，因此不适用于安全关键应用。相反，形式化综合技术提供“正确性由构造保证”，但通常面临可扩展性问题，因为一般POMDP综合问题是不可判定的。为弥补这一差距，我们提出了一种集成抽样、自动机学习与模型检测的综合框架。受Angluin的$L^*$算法启发，我们的方法将抽样作为成员查询预言，将模型检测作为等价查询预言。这使得我们能够在抽样诱导的策略是正则的前提下，综合出具有形式化保证的有限状态控制器。我们为该框架建立了相对完备性结果。我们原型实现的实验结果表明，该方法成功解决了现有形式化综合工具仍难以处理的阈值安全问题。我们相信，我们的算法可作为解决POMDP综合问题固有难度的一种组合方法中的有价值组件。

Original abstract: Partially Observable Markov Decision Processes (POMDPs) are the standard framework for decision-making under uncertainty. While sampling-based methods scale well, they lack formal correctness guarantees, making them unsuitable for safety-critical applications. Conversely, formal synthesis techniques provide correctness-by-construction but often struggle with scalability, as general POMDP synthesis is undecidable. To bridge this gap, we propose a synthesis framework that integrates sampling, automata learning, and model-checking. Inspired by Angluin's $L^*$ algorithm, our approach utilizes sampling as a membership oracle and model-checking as an equivalence oracle. This enables the synthesis of finite-state controllers with formal guarantees, provided the sampling-induced policy is regular. We establish a relative completeness result for this framework. Experimental results from our prototypical implementation demonstrate that this method successfully solves threshold-safety problems that remain challenging for existing formal synthesis tools. We believe our algorithm serves as a valuable component in a portfolio approach to tackling the inherent difficulty of POMDP synthesis problems.

### [34] [Prompting Policies for Multi-step Reasoning and Tool-Use in Black-box LLMs with Iterative Distillation of Experience](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14443v1)

Result: 在BBEH和Tau-bench上，逻辑推理准确率从55%提升至90%，工具使用任务从74%提升至91%，且样本效率高于GEPA等基线。

Conclusion: 迭代蒸馏策略能有效学习提示优化，发现专门算法启发式，且性能与样本效率优于进化方法。

中文摘要：与冻结的“黑盒”大型语言模型（LLM）交互的转变，已使提示工程从一种启发式练习转变为一项关键的优化挑战。我们提出了一种基于强化学习（RL）的框架，通过经验的迭代蒸馏来训练学习到的提示策略。在该架构中，一个轻量级的提示器模型被优化，以最大化一个更大的、冻结的工作LLM的任务特定奖励。通过利用将标量奖励与密集文本批评相结合的对比经验缓冲区，我们的方法有效地将迭代提示优化摊销到单次策略权重中。我们的实验分析聚焦于Big Bench Extra Hard (BBEH)和Tau-bench套件，涵盖多种多步推理和工具使用任务。我们展示了显著的收益，在逻辑密集推理中性能从55%提升到90%，在工具使用任务中从74%提升到91%。此外，我们分析了提示的结构演化，展示了策略如何发现专门的算法启发式。我们与最先进的进化基线（如GEPA）进行了全面比较，表明迭代蒸馏在更高样本效率下实现了优越的性能。

Original abstract: The shift toward interacting with frozen, "black-box" Large Language Models (LLMs) has transformed prompt engineering from a heuristic exercise into a critical optimization challenge. We propose a Reinforcement Learning (RL) framework for training learned prompting policies via iterative distillation of experience. In this architecture, a lightweight prompter model is optimized to maximize task-specific rewards for a larger, frozen worker LLM. By utilizing a contrastive experience buffer that couples scalar rewards with dense textual critiques, our approach effectively amortizes iterative prompt refinement into single-shot policy weights.
  Our experimental analysis focuses on the Big Bench Extra Hard (BBEH) and Tau-bench suites, covering a diverse range of multi-step reasoning and tool-use tasks. We demonstrate significant gains, improving performance from 55% to 90% in logic-intensive reasoning and 74% to 91% in tool-use tasks. Furthermore, we analyze the structural evolution of prompts, demonstrating how the policy discovers specialized algorithmic heuristics. We provide comprehensive comparisons against state-of-the-art evolutionary baselines like GEPA, showing that iterative distillation achieves superior performance with higher sample efficiency.

</details>


### [35] [Stateful Reasoning via Insight Replay](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14457v2)
*Bin Lei,Caiwen Ding,Jiachen Yang,Ang Li,Xin Eric Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出InsightReplay提升长链推理的洞察可访问性，对agent状态推理有直接价值。

TL;DR: 提出InsightReplay方法，通过定期提取并重放推理轨迹中的关键见解，缓解长链推理中注意力衰减问题，在24个设置上平均提升1.65个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长链思维推理中，模型对早期关键见解的注意力随链长增加而减弱，导致准确率先升后降，需要提升长推理轨迹中关键信息的可访问性。

Method: InsightReplay：一种有状态推理方法，模型周期性从推理轨迹中提取关键见解，并将其重放到当前生成前沿附近，确保在扩展推理时关键信息保持可用。

Result: 在2×3×4基准网格（8B/30B规模、三个模型族、四个基准）上，3轮InsightReplay在所有24个设置中均提升准确率，平均提升+1.65点，最大单设置提升+9.2点。

Conclusion: 测试时扩展的有效性不仅取决于推理量，还取决于长推理轨迹中关键中间见解的可访问性。

中文摘要：链式思维（CoT）推理已成为激发大语言模型多步推理的基础，但近期研究表明，其收益并不随链长单调递增：虽然更长的CoT通常使模型能够处理更困难的问题，但对于给定问题，准确率通常随CoT长度增加而上升至某一点，随后下降。我们识别出这一现象的一个主要原因：随着CoT增长，模型对推理轨迹早期产生的关键见解的注意力逐渐减弱，使得这些见解在最需要时变得愈发难以获取。因此，我们提出InsightReplay，一种有状态推理方法，其中模型定期从其推理轨迹中提取关键见解，并将其重放到活跃生成前沿附近，从而在推理扩展时保持这些见解的可访问性。在涵盖模型规模{8B, 30B}、模型系列{Qwen3.5, DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen, Gemma-4}以及推理基准{AIME, HMMT, GPQA Diamond, LiveCodeBench v5}的2×3×4基准网格上进行的广泛实验表明，3轮InsightReplay在所有24个设置中均带来了准确率提升，相较于标准CoT平均提升+1.65个百分点，最大单设置提升出现在R1-Distill-32B的LiveCodeBench v5子集上，为+9.2个百分点。我们的结果表明，测试时扩展的有效性不仅取决于模型推理了多少，还取决于关键中间见解在长推理轨迹中是否保持可访问。

Original abstract: Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning has become a foundation for eliciting multi-step reasoning in large language models, but recent studies show that its benefits do not scale monotonically with chain length: while longer CoT generally enables a model to tackle harder problems, on a given problem, accuracy typically increases with CoT length up to a point, after which it declines. We identify a major cause of this phenomenon: as the CoT grows, the model's attention to critical insights produced earlier in the trace gradually weakens, making those insights progressively less accessible when they are most needed. Therefore, we propose \textbf{InsightReplay}, a stateful reasoning approach in which the model periodically extracts critical insights from its reasoning trace and replays them near the active generation frontier, keeping them accessible as the reasoning scales. Extensive experiments on a $\mathbf{2}\!\times\!\mathbf{3}\!\times\!\mathbf{4}$ benchmark grid, covering model scales $\{\text{8B}, \text{30B}\}$, model families $\{\text{Qwen3.5}, \text{DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen}, \text{Gemma-4}\}$, and reasoning benchmarks $\{\text{AIME}, \text{HMMT}, \text{GPQA Diamond}, \text{LiveCodeBench v5}\}$, show that 3-round InsightReplay yields accuracy gains across \textbf{all 24 settings}, with an averaged improvement of $\mathbf{+1.65}$ points over standard CoT, and a largest single-setting gain of $\mathbf{+9.2}$ points on R1-Distill-32B's LiveCodeBench v5 subset. Our results suggest that the effectiveness of test-time scaling depends not only on how much a model reasons, but also on whether critical intermediate insights remain accessible throughout long reasoning trajectories.

### [36] [From Table to Cell: Attention for Better Reasoning with TABALIGN](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14465v1)
*Tung Sum Thomas Kwok,Zeyong Zhang,Xinyu Wang,Chunhe Wang,Xiaofeng Lin,Hanwei Wu,Lei Ding,Guang Cheng,Zhijiang Guo*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 采用diffusion planner和轻量验证器进行表格推理，planner-verifier架构可迁移至agent。

TL;DR: 提出TABALIGN框架，利用扩散语言模型规划器实现更稳定和高效的表格推理，在多项基准上显著提升准确率和速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多步LLM表格推理中，规划与执行缺乏显式单元格级基础契约，现有方法受限于从左到右的因子分解且忽略单元格级基础，导致性能不佳。

Method: 提出TABALIGN框架，包含掩码DLM规划器（通过双向去噪生成二进制单元格掩码作为计划步骤）和TABATTN验证器（基于人工验证注意力标准评分计划步骤的注意力重叠）。

Result: 在八个基准上平均准确率提升15.76个百分点（对比最强开源8B模型），消融实验证实DLM规划器贡献2.87个百分点，且推理速度提升44.64%。

Conclusion: 扩散语言模型在表格推理中具有优势，TABALIGN通过显式单元格级基础契约显著提升准确率和效率。

中文摘要：多步LLM在结构化表格上的推理失败，因为规划和执行之间缺乏明确的单元格级基础契约。现有方法将规划器限制为从左到右的因子分解，与表格的排列不变性相悖，并且仅根据生成内容对中间状态进行评分，忽略了单元格级基础。我们进行了一项初步研究，表明扩散语言模型（DLM）在表格上产生的单元格注意力比自回归模型更符合人类对齐且排列稳定，在行重排序下注意力-AUROC变异性中位数降低40.2%。受此启发，我们提出了TABALIGN，这是一个实现该契约的规划式表格推理框架。TABALIGN将一个掩码DLM规划器与TABATTN配对，前者通过双向去噪发出作为二进制单元格掩码的计划步骤，后者是一个轻量级验证器，在1,600个人工验证的注意力标准上训练，通过每个步骤的注意力与计划指定掩码的重叠度进行评分。在涵盖表格问答和事实验证的八个基准测试中，TABALIGN在可比的8B类规模上将平均准确率比最强的开源基线提高了15.76个百分点，一个匹配主干的消融实验将其中2.87个百分点的增益归因于固定推理器上DLM规划器相对于AR规划器。更清晰的DLM计划还加速了下游推理执行44.64%。

Original abstract: Multi-step LLM reasoning over structured tables fails because planning and execution share no explicit cell-grounding contract. Existing methods constrain the planner to a left-to-right factorization at odds with table permutation invariance, and score intermediate states by generated content alone, overlooking cell grounding. We conduct a pilot study showing that diffusion language models (DLMs) produce more human-aligned and permutation-stable cell attention on tables than autoregressive models, with a 40.2% median reduction in attention-AUROC variability under row reordering. Motivated by this, we propose TABALIGN, a planned table reasoning framework that operationalizes the contract. TABALIGN pairs a masked DLM planner, whose bidirectional denoising emits plan steps as binary cell masks, with TABATTN, a lightweight verifier trained on 1,600 human-verified attention standards to score each step by its attention overlap with the plan-designated mask. Across eight benchmarks covering table question answering and fact verification, TABALIGN improves average accuracy by 15.76 percentage points over the strongest open-source baseline at comparable 8B-class scale, with a matched-backbone ablation attributing 2.87 percentage points of this gain to the DLM planner over an AR planner on a fixed reasoner. Cleaner DLM plans also accelerate downstream reasoning execution by 44.64%.

### [37] [LEMON: Learning Executable Multi-Agent Orchestration via Counterfactual Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14483v1)
*Xudong Chen,Yixin Liu,Hua Wei,Kaize Ding*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 利用反事实强化学习自动学习多agent编排，直接贡献agent架构与训练方法。

TL;DR: LEMON是一种基于LLM的多智能体编排方法，通过反事实强化学习优化角色、能力和依赖设计，在多个基准上达到SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有编排设计方法部分或顺序优化决策，且依赖执行级反馈，难以对局部编排决策进行有效信用分配。

Method: 提出LEMON，采用增强的GRPO目标，通过编辑角色、能力或依赖字段并应用局部反事实奖励对比来训练编排器。

Result: 在MMLU、GSM8K、AQuA、MultiArith、SVAMP和HumanEval六个基准上取得最佳性能。

Conclusion: LEMON通过反事实强化学习有效提升了多智能体编排的性能和执行效率。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）已成为多智能体系统的坚实基础，但其有效性高度依赖于编排设计。在不同任务中，角色设计、能力分配和依赖关系构建共同影响解决方案质量和执行效率。现有方法自动化了部分设计过程，但往往部分或顺序地优化这些决策，并依赖于执行级反馈，这种反馈对局部编排决策的信用分配有限。我们提出LEMON（基于反事实强化学习的可执行多智能体编排学习），一种基于LLM的编排器，可生成可执行的编排规范。该规范将特定任务的角色、自定义职责、能力水平和依赖结构集成到单个可部署系统中。为了训练编排器，我们使用局部反事实信号增强编排级GRPO目标，该信号编辑角色、能力或依赖字段，并将生成的奖励对比仅应用于编辑的跨度。在六个推理和编码基准（包括MMLU、GSM8K、AQuA、MultiArith、SVAMP和HumanEval）上的实验表明，LEMON在评估的多智能体编排方法中达到了最先进的性能。我们的代码可在https://anonymous.4open.science/r/LEMON-B23C获取。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have become a strong foundation for multi-agent systems, but their effectiveness depends heavily on orchestration design. Across different tasks, role design, capacity assignment, and dependency construction jointly affect both solution quality and execution efficiency. Existing approaches automate parts of this design process, yet they often optimize these decisions partially or sequentially, and rely on execution-level feedback that provides limited credit assignment for local orchestration decisions. We propose LEMON (\textbf{L}earning \textbf{E}xecutable \textbf{M}ulti-agent \textbf{O}rchestratio\textbf{N} via Counterfactual Reinforcement Learning), an LLM-based orchestrator that generates an executable orchestration specification. The specification integrates task-specific roles, customized duties, capacity levels, and dependency structure into a single deployable system. To train the orchestrator, we augment the orchestration-level GRPO objective with a localized counterfactual signal that edits role, capacity, or dependency fields and applies the resulting reward contrast only to the edited spans. Experiments on six reasoning and coding benchmarks, including MMLU, GSM8K, AQuA, MultiArith, SVAMP, and HumanEval, show that LEMON achieves state-of-the-art performance among the evaluated multi-agent orchestration methods. Our code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/LEMON-B23C.

</details>

### [39] [When Robots Do the Chores: A Benchmark and Agent for Long-Horizon Household Task Execution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14504v2)

Original abstract: Long-horizon household tasks demand robust high-level planning and sustained reasoning capabilities, which are largely overlooked by existing embodied AI benchmarks that emphasize short-horizon navigation or manipulation and rely on fixed task categories. We introduce LongAct, a benchmark designed to evaluate planning-level autonomy in long-horizon household tasks specified through free-form instructions. By abstracting away embodiment-specific low-level control, LongAct isolates high-level cognitive capabilities such as instruction understanding, dependency management, memory maintenance, and adaptive planning. We further propose HoloMind, a VLM-driven agent with a DAG-based long-horizon hierarchical planner, a Multimodal Spatial Memory for persistent world modeling, an Episodic Memory for experience reuse, and a global Critic for reflective supervision. Experiments with GPT-5 and Qwen3-VL models show that HoloMind substantially improves long-horizon performance while reducing reliance on model scale. ### [40] [Cattle Trade: A Multi-Agent Benchmark for LLM Bluffing, Bidding, and Bargaining](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14537v1)
*Robert Müller,Clemens Müller*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多Agent博弈基准，含欺骗、竞价、谈判，评估多能力联合部署，直接相关

TL;DR: Cattle Trade 是一个多智能体经济游戏基准测试，用于评估LLM在战略推理中的综合能力，发现启发式代码智能体优于多数LLM，且战略连贯性比单一技能更重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试孤立地测试战略推理中的各个子技能，缺乏在竞争性、多智能体且激励冲突的环境中整合这些能力的评估。

Method: 设计了一个包含拍卖、隐藏交易、议价、虚张声势和资源分配的多轮经济游戏，记录所有行为数据，并在242场游戏中评估了7个LLM和3个代码智能体。

Result: 两个启发式代码智能体优于多数LLM；战略连贯性（支出效率、资源纪律、阶段自适应出价）与排名强相关；LLM常见失败包括过度出价、自我出价、破产TC发起和对手状态适应弱。

Conclusion: 评估智能体能力需要能够测试多种能力联合部署的基准测试，特别是在激励冲突、不确定性和经济动态的多智能体环境中。

中文摘要：我们介绍了 Cattle Trade，这是一个多智能体基准测试，用于评估大型语言模型（LLM）作为智能体在不完全信息、对抗性交互和资源约束下的战略推理能力。该基准测试将拍卖、隐藏报价交易挑战（TC）、议价、虚张声势、对手建模和资源分配整合在一个持续50-60回合的长周期游戏中。与先前孤立测试这些能力的智能体基准测试不同，Cattle Trade 评估智能体是否能够在竞争性、多智能体且激励冲突的经济游戏中整合这些能力。基准测试记录每一次出价、TC报价、还价和卡牌选择，从而能够进行超越最终得分或胜率的行为分析。我们在242场游戏中评估了七个成本高效的语言模型和三个确定性代码智能体。战略连贯性，特别是支出效率、资源纪律和阶段自适应出价，与排名的关联强于支出量或任何单一子技能。两个启发式代码智能体表现优于大多数测试的LLM，行为痕迹揭示了LLM反复出现的失败模式，包括过度出价、自我出价、破产TC发起和对手状态适应薄弱。评估智能体能力需要测试在具有激励冲突、不确定性和经济动态的多智能体环境中联合部署多种能力的基准测试。

Original abstract: We introduce \textsc{Cattle Trade, a multi-agent benchmark for evaluating large language models (LLMs) as agents in strategic reasoning under imperfect information, adversarial interaction, and resource constraints. The benchmark combines auctions, hidden-offer trade challenges (TCs), bargaining, bluffing, opponent modeling, and resource allocation within a single long-horizon game lasting 50--60 turns. Unlike prior agent benchmarks that test these abilities in isolation, \textsc{Cattle Trade} evaluates whether agents integrate them across a competitive, multi-agent economic game with conflicting incentives. The benchmark logs every bid, TC offer, counteroffer, and card selection, enabling behavioural analysis beyond final scores or win rates. We evaluate seven cost-efficient language models and three deterministic code agents across 242 games. Strategic coherence, in particular spending efficiency, resource discipline, and phase-adaptive bidding, is associated with rank more strongly than spending volume or any single subskill. Two heuristic code agents outperform most tested LLMs, and behavioural traces surface recurring LLM failure modes including overbidding, self-bidding, bankrupt TC initiation, and weak opponent-state adaptation. Evaluating agentic competence requires benchmarks that test the joint deployment of multiple capabilities in multi-agent environments with conflicting incentives, uncertainty, and economic dynamics.

Building on this paradigm, we developed TeachAnything, a cloud-based, crowdsourcing-oriented demonstration platform with physics simulation capable of collecting diverse demonstration data across varied scenes, tasks, and embodiments. By unifying virtual and physical interactions through both methodological design and physics simulation, the system serves as a practical foundation for developing embodied agents aligned with Symmetrical Reality.

### [42] [Prompt Segmentation and Annotation Optimisation: Controlling LLM Behaviour via Optimised Segment-Level Annotations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14561v1)
*Devika Prasad,Luke Gerschwitz,Tong Li,Henry Xiao,Anjin Liu,Coco Wu,Anna Leontjeva,Luiz Pizzato*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提示分段注释优化，可辅助Agent提示工程，但贡献有限

TL;DR: 提出PSAO框架，通过将提示分解为带注释的片段，提高LLM推理准确性和自一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有提示优化方法计算成本高、易扭曲原始意图，需要更可控高效的优化方法。

Method: 将提示分解为可解释片段并添加重要性注释，引导LLM分配注意力，同时保留原始提示作为候选。

Result: 在推理准确性和自一致性上取得提升。

Conclusion: 概念验证表明片段级注释优化可行，但高效获取最优分割和注释的方法仍需未来研究。

中文摘要：提示工程对于与生成式人工智能系统的有效交互至关重要，然而现有的优化方法通常在一个非结构化和庞大的提示空间上运行，导致高计算成本和原始意图的潜在扭曲。我们引入了提示分割与注释优化（PSAO），一个结构化的提示优化框架，旨在提高提示优化的可控性和效率。PSAO将提示分解为可解释的片段（例如句子），并为每个片段增加人类可读的注释（例如，{不重要}，{重要}，{非常重要}）。这些注释指导大型语言模型（LLMs）在生成响应时分配注意力并澄清困惑。我们正式定义了分割和注释，并证明了优化的片段级注释可以改善LLM的响应，同时保留原始提示作为优化空间中的候选，以防止性能下降。实证评估表明，PSAO从注释中受益，提高了推理准确性和自一致性。然而，开发识别最优分割和注释的高效方法仍然具有挑战性，留待未来研究。本工作旨在作为概念验证，展示片段级注释优化的可行性和潜力。

Original abstract: Prompt engineering is crucial for effective interaction with generative artificial intelligence systems, yet existing optimisation methods often operate over an unstructured and vast prompt space, leading to high computational costs and potential distortions of the original intent. We introduce Prompt Segmentation and Annotation Optimisation (PSAO), a structured prompt optimisation framework designed to improve prompt optimisation controllability and efficiency. PSAO decomposes a prompt into interpretable segments (e.g., sentences) and augments each with human-readable annotations (e.g., {not important}, {important}, {very important}). These annotations guide large language models (LLMs) in allocating focus and clarifying confusion during response generation. We formally define the segmentations and annotations and demonstrate that optimised segment-level annotations can lead to improved LLM responses, with the original prompt retained as a candidate in the optimisation space to prevent performance degradation. Empirical evaluations indicate that PSAO benefits from annotations in terms of improved reasoning accuracy and self-consistency. However, developing efficient methods for identifying optimal segmentations and annotations remains challenging and is reserved for future investigation. This work is intended as a proof of concept, demonstrating the feasibility and potential of segment-level annotation optimisation.

### [43] [Teaching Large Language Models When Not to Know: Learning Temporal Critique for Ex-Ante Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14636v1)
*Chenlu Ding,Jiancan Wu,Yanchen Luo,Zheyuan Liu,Yancheng Yuan,Xiang Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 时间批评微调框架，训练模型进行验证，可迁移到agent自我反思

TL;DR: 提出TCFT框架，通过时间批评微调训练模型识别并避免时间截断后的知识泄漏，在Qwen2.5模型上显著优于提示和SFT基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在时间截断推理中常利用未来知识，现有提示和微调方法不足以让模型获得验证时间合规性的能力。

Method: 提出Temporal Critique Fine-Tuning（TCFT）框架，给定查询、截断和候选响应，训练模型识别后截断泄漏、解释时间边界违规并判断时间可接受性。

Result: 在Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct和Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct上，TCFT相比提示和SFT基线分别减少平均泄漏41.89和37.79个百分点。

Conclusion: TCFT能有效提升模型对时间截断的遵守能力，表明通过时间批评微调可以弥补现有方法在时间验证上的不足。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）常常在时间截断条件下推理失败：当被提示从较早时间点的立场回答时，它们会利用后来才可获得的知识。我们通过事前推理的视角研究这一失败，其中模型必须仅依赖截断前可知的信息。通过对提示层面干预的系统分析，我们发现时间泄漏对截断表述和指令放置高度敏感：显式截断语句优于隐式历史框架，前缀约束比后缀约束更能有效减少泄漏。这些发现表明，提示能够引导模型进入一个时间框架，但并不能赋予模型验证响应是否时间上可接受的能力。我们进一步论证监督微调是不足够的，因为事前正确性并非答案的内在属性，而是答案与截断之间的关系。为弥补这一差距，我们提出了TCFT，一种时间批评微调框架，训练模型获得对截断感知的时间验证能力。给定一个查询、一个截断和一个候选响应，TCFT教导模型识别截断后泄漏、解释时间边界违规并判断时间可接受性。在Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct和Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct上的实验表明，TCFT在减少平均泄漏方面持续优于提示和SFT基线，分别降低了41.89和37.79个百分点。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) often fail to reason under temporal cutoffs: when prompted to answer from the standpoint of an earlier time, they exploit knowledge that became available only later. We study this failure through the lens of ex-ante reasoning, where a model must rely exclusively on information knowable before a cutoff. Through a systematic analysis of prompt-level interventions, we find that temporal leakage is highly sensitive to cutoff formulation and instruction placement: explicit cutoff statements outperform implicit historical framings, and prefix constraints reduce leakage more effectively than suffix constraints. These findings indicate that prompting can steer models into a temporal frame, but does not endow them with the ability to verify whether a response is temporally admissible. We further argue that supervised fine-tuning is insufficient, since ex-ante correctness is not an intrinsic property of an answer, but a relation between the answer and the cutoff. To address this gap, we propose TCFT, a Temporal Critique Fine-Tuning framework that trains models to acquire cutoff-aware temporal verification. Given a query, a cutoff, and a candidate response, TCFT teaches the model to identify post-cutoff leakage, explain temporal boundary violations, and judge temporal admissibility. Experiments with Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct and Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct show that TCFT consistently outperforms prompting and SFT baselines, reducing average leakage by 41.89 and 37.79 percentage points, respectively.

</details>


### [44] [Falkor-IRAC: Graph-Constrained Generation for Verified Legal Reasoning in Indian Judicial AI](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14665v2)
*Joy Bose*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 法律推理的图约束生成与verifier agent，可迁移到代码生成验证

TL;DR: Falkor-IRAC是一个图约束生成框架，利用IRAC知识图谱和验证器智能体减少LLM在法律推理中的虚构和错误，适用于印度法律AI。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于向量的RAG无法忠实表示法律推理中的符号约束，导致LLM产生虚构先例和错误引用，影响司法公正；需要更可靠的生成框架。

Method: 将判决构建为IRAC知识图谱（含程序状态、先例、法规引用），使用FalkorDB存储；推理时LLM答案需通过验证器智能体在图中的路径检查，并检测教义冲突。

Result: 在51个判决的测试中，验证器正确验证真实引用、拒绝虚构引用；图原生指标更合适，但尚未与向量RAG基线对比。

Conclusion: Falkor-IRAC通过图约束和验证机制提升了法律推理的可靠性，但需进一步评估；开源InIRAC数据集促进研究。

中文摘要：法律推理并不是语义相似性搜索。法院判决编码了受约束的符号推理：先例传播、程序状态转换和法规约束的推理。这些都是基于向量的检索增强生成（RAG）无法忠实表示的属性。在基于LLM的法律AI中，虚构的先例、过时的法规引用以及无依据的推理链仍然是持续存在的失败模式，这对于印度等高案件量司法管辖区的诉诸司法机会产生了实际影响。本文提出了Falkor-IRAC，一个针对印度法律AI的图约束生成框架，该框架将生成过程建立在IRAC（问题、规则、分析、结论）知识图谱上的结构化推理之上。来自印度最高法院和高等法院的判决被提取为IRAC节点结构，并丰富了程序状态转换、先例关系和法定引用，存储在FalkorDB中，以实现低延迟的智能体遍历。在推理时，只有当可以通过图追踪到有效的支持路径时，LLM生成的答案才被接受，这一检查由名为验证器智能体的可证伪性预言机执行。该系统还将教义冲突作为一等输出进行检测，而不是默默解决。Falkor-IRAC使用图原生指标进行评估：引用基础准确率、路径有效比率、虚构先例率和冲突检测率。这些指标被认为比BLEU和ROUGE更适合法律推理评估。在一个包含51个最高法院判决的概念验证语料库上，验证器智能体正确验证了已完成查询的引用，并正确拒绝了虚构引用。与仅向量的RAG基线的评估留待未来工作。伴随本文发布的还有InIRAC数据集，包含500多个结构化的印度法院判决以及IRAC注释。

Original abstract: Legal reasoning is not semantic similarity search. A court judgment encodes constrained symbolic reasoning: precedent propagation, procedural state transitions, and statute-bound inference. These are properties that vector-based retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) cannot faithfully represent. Hallucinated precedents, outdated statute citations, and unsupported reasoning chains remain persistent failure modes in LLM-based legal AI, with real consequences for access to justice in high-caseload jurisdictions such as India. This paper presents Falkor-IRAC, a graph-constrained generation framework for Indian legal AI that grounds generation in structured reasoning over an IRAC (Issue, Rule, Analysis, Conclusion) knowledge graph. Judgments from the Supreme Court and High Courts of India are ingested as IRAC node structures enriched with procedural state transitions, precedent relationships, and statutory references, stored in FalkorDB for low-latency agentic traversal. At inference time, LLM-generated answers are accepted only if a valid supporting path can be traced through the graph, a check performed by a falsifiability oracle called the Verifier Agent. The system also detects doctrinal conflicts as a first-class output rather than silently resolving them. Falkor-IRAC is evaluated using graph-native metrics: citation grounding accuracy, path validity rate, hallucinated precedent rate, and conflict detection rate. These metrics are argued to be more appropriate for legal reasoning evaluation than BLEU and ROUGE. On a proof-of-concept corpus of 51 Supreme Court judgments, the Verifier Agent correctly validated citations on completed queries and correctly rejected fabricated citations. Evaluation against vector-only RAG baselines is left for future work. The companion InIRAC dataset, 500+ structured Indian court judgments with IRAC annotations, is released alongside this paper.

</details>


### [45] [$π$-Bench: Evaluating Proactive Personal Assistant Agents in Long-Horizon Workflows](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14678v3)
*Haoran Zhang,Luxin Xu,Zhilin Wang,Runquan Gui,Shunkai Zhang,Haodi Lei,Zihao He,Bingsu He,Chicheng Qin,Tong Zhu,Xiaoye Qu,Yang Yang,Yu Cheng,Yafu Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出π-Bench，评估长期工作流中主动助手的隐藏意图推理，对agent评测和长期任务有参考价值。

TL;DR: 提出π-Bench基准测试，评估智能体在长时间多轮交互中主动识别并满足用户未明确表述意图的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试很少评估智能体在用户需求未明确表述时主动识别并行动的能力，尤其是在多轮交互中。

Method: 构建包含5个用户画像、100个多轮任务的π-Bench，通过隐藏意图、任务依赖和跨会话连续性模拟真实场景。

Result: 主动协助仍具挑战；任务完成与主动性存在明显区别；先前交互有助于后续任务的主动意图解决。

Conclusion: π-Bench有效评估了智能体的主动协助能力，揭示了当前模型的不足及历史交互的价值。

中文摘要：个人助手智能体的兴起，例如OpenClaw，突显了大型语言模型在支持用户日常和生活工作中的巨大潜力。这类设置中的一个核心挑战是主动协助，因为用户通常以未明确表述的请求开始，并留下重要的需求、约束或偏好未说明。然而，现有的基准测试很少评估智能体能否在用户明确表述之前识别并采取行动处理这些隐藏意图，尤其是在用户需求逐渐浮现的持续多轮交互中。为了填补这一空白，我们引入了π-Bench，一个用于主动协助的基准测试，包含5个领域特定用户画像下的100个多轮任务。通过整合隐藏的用户意图、任务间依赖性以及跨会话连续性，π-Bench评估了智能体在扩展交互中预判和满足用户需求的能力，共同衡量了长期轨迹中的主动性和任务完成情况，更好地反映了实际使用情况。实验表明（1）主动协助仍然具有挑战性，（2）任务完成与主动性之间存在明显区别，以及（3）先前交互对于在后续任务中主动解决意图的价值。

Original abstract: The rise of personal assistant agents, e.g., OpenClaw, highlights the growing potential of large language models to support users across everyday life and work. A core challenge in these settings is proactive assistance, since users often begin with underspecified requests and leave important needs, constraints, or preferences unstated. However, existing benchmarks rarely evaluate whether agents can identify and act on such hidden intents before they are explicitly stated, especially in sustained multi-turn interactions where user needs emerge gradually. To address this gap, we introduce $π$-Bench, a benchmark for proactive assistance comprising 100 multi-turn tasks across 5 domain-specific user personas. By incorporating hidden user intents, inter-task dependencies, and cross-session continuity, $π$-Bench evaluates agents' ability to anticipate and address user needs over extended interactions, jointly measuring proactivity and task completion in long-horizon trajectories that better reflect real-world use. Experiments show (1) proactive assistance remains challenging, (2) a clear distinction between task completion and proactivity, and (3) the value of prior interaction for proactive intent resolution in later tasks.

### [46] [Agentifying Patient Dynamics within LLMs through Interacting with Clinical World Model](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14723v1)
*Minghao Wu,Yuting Yan,Zhenyang Cai,Ke Ji,Chuangsen Fang,Ziying Sheng,Xidong Wang,Rongsheng Wang,Hejia Zhang,Shuang Li,Benyou Wang,Hongyuan Zha*

TL;DR: SepsisAgent通过结合临床世界模型和LLM，在脓毒症治疗推荐中显著优于传统方法和LLM基线，并具有最佳安全性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM缺乏对行动条件患者动态的固有理解，导致决策不一致，因此需要引入世界模型和专门训练来提升脓毒症治疗决策的可靠性和安全性。

Method: 提出SepsisAgent，包含一个临床世界模型（模拟患者对干预的反应）和一个LLM，通过三阶段训练（患者动态监督微调、提出-模拟-优化行为克隆、基于世界模型的强化学习）来学习治疗策略。

Result: 在MIMIC-IV数据集上，SepsisAgent在离策略价值、指南依从性和不安全行动指标上均优于所有基线（包括传统RL和LLM方法）。

Conclusion: 与临床世界模型的重复交互使智能体能够学习患者演化规律，即使没有模拟器也能保持有效，表明世界模型增强的LLM智能体在ICU决策中具有潜力。

中文摘要：在ICU中，脓毒症管理需要在快速变化的患者生理状态下进行序贯治疗决策。尽管大型语言模型（LLM）编码了广泛的临床知识并能推理指南，但它们本质上并未基于行动条件的患者动态。我们引入了SepsisAgent，一种世界模型增强的LLM智能体，用于脓毒症治疗推荐。SepsisAgent使用学习的临床世界模型来模拟候选液体-血管加压药干预下的患者反应，并在最终开具处方前遵循提出-模拟-优化的流程。我们首先表明，仅通过世界模型访问会导致LLM决策性能不一致，从而激励了智能体特定的训练。然后我们通过三阶段课程训练SepsisAgent：患者动态监督微调、提出-模拟-优化行为克隆以及基于世界模型的智能体强化学习。在MIMIC-IV脓毒症轨迹上，SepsisAgent在离策略价值上优于所有传统RL和基于LLM的基线，同时在指南依从性和不安全行动指标下实现最佳安全特性。进一步分析表明，与临床世界模型的重复交互使智能体能够学习患者演化的规律，即使在移除模拟器访问时这些规律仍然有用。

Original abstract: Sepsis management in the ICU requires sequential treatment decisions under rapidly evolving patient physiology. Although large language models (LLMs) encode broad clinical knowledge and can reason over guidelines, they are not inherently grounded in action-conditioned patient dynamics. We introduce SepsisAgent, a world model-augmented LLM agent for sepsis treatment recommendation. SepsisAgent uses a learned Clinical World Model to simulate patient responses under candidate fluid--vasopressor interventions, and follows a propose--simulate--refine workflow before committing to a prescription. We first show that world-model access alone yields inconsistent LLM decision performance, motivating agent-specific training. We then train SepsisAgent through a three-stage curriculum: patient-dynamics supervised fine-tuning, propose--simulate--refine behavior cloning, and world-model-based agentic reinforcement learning. On MIMIC-IV sepsis trajectories, SepsisAgent outperforms all traditional RL and LLM-based baselines in off-policy value while achieving the best safety profile under guideline adherence and unsafe-action metrics. Further analysis shows that repeated interaction with the Clinical World Model enables the agent to learn regularities in patient evolution, which remain useful even when simulator access is removed.

### [47] [XDomainBench: Diagnosing Reasoning Collapse in High-Dimensional Scientific Knowledge Composition](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14754v1)
*Gong Zhiren,Tiantong Wu,Jiaming Zhang,Fuyao Zhang,Che Wang,Yurong Hao,Yikun Hou,Foo Ping,Yilei Zhao,Fei Huang,Chau Yuen,Wei Yang Bryan Lim*

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed for knowledge synthesis, yet their capacity for compositional generalization in scientific knowledge remains under-characterized. Existing benchmarks primarily focus on single-turn restricted scenarios, failing to capture the capability boundaries exposed by real-world interactive scientific workflows. To address this, we introduce XDomainBench, a diagnostic benchmark for interactive interdisciplinary scientific reasoning. We formalize the composition order and mixture structure to enable systematic stress-testing from single-discipline to inter-disciplinary, comprising 8,598 interactive sessions across 20 domains and 4 task categories, with 8 realistic trajectory patterns covering difficulty and domain-mixture dynamics, simulating real AI4S scenarios. Large-scale evaluation of LLMs reveals a systematic reasoning collapse as composition order increases, stemming from two root causes: (i) direct difficulty increases induced by domain composition, and (ii) indirect interaction-amplified failures where trajectory patterns trigger error accumulation, reasoning breaks, and domain confusion, ultimately leading to session collapse.

### [48] [Probabilistic Verification of Recurrent Neural Networks for Single and Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14758v1)
*Luca Marzari,Enrico Marchesini*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: RNN策略概率验证框架，对多agent系统可靠性验证有启发。

TL;DR: 提出RNN-ProVe，一个概率验证框架，通过策略驱动采样和统计误差界限估计RNN策略中不良行为的可能性，在部分可观测RL任务上提供更定量和可行的保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的RNN验证工具由于依赖限制性假设或粗略过近似，导致结果过于保守或不确定，无法有效验证部分可观测RL中的RNN策略。

Method: 提出RNN-ProVe框架，使用策略驱动采样近似训练策略下可行的隐状态集，并推导统计误差界限，以产生有界误差、高置信度的行为违规概率估计。

Result: 在部分可观测单智能体和合作多智能体任务上，RNN-ProVe比现有工具提供了更定量、更可行性感知的概率保证，并能扩展到循环和多智能体设置。

Conclusion: RNN-ProVe是一种有效的概率验证方法，能够在实际RNN策略上提供有保证的可靠性估计，克服了传统验证工具的局限性。

中文摘要：由循环神经网络（RNN）驱动的历史依赖策略依赖于隐状态动态，这使得部分可观测强化学习（RL）中的验证变得具有挑战性。现有的RNN验证工具通常依赖于限制性的建模假设或隐状态空间的粗略过近似，这可能导致过于保守或不确定的结果。我们提出了RNN概率验证（RNN-ProVe），一个概率框架，用于估计RNN策略中不良行为的可能性。RNN-ProVe使用策略驱动采样来近似在训练策略下可行的隐状态集合，并推导统计误差界限以产生有界误差、高置信度的行为违规估计。在部分可观测单智能体和合作多智能体任务上的实验表明，RNN-ProVe比现有工具产生了更定量、更可行的概率保证，同时扩展到循环和多智能体设置。

Original abstract: History-dependent policies induced by recurrent neural networks (RNNs) rely on latent hidden state dynamics, making verification in partially observable reinforcement learning (RL) challenging. Existing RNN verification tools typically rely on restrictive modeling assumptions or coarse over-approximations of the hidden state space, which can lead to overly conservative or inconclusive results. We propose $\textbf{RNN}$ $\textbf{Pro}$babilistic $\textbf{Ve}$rification ($\texttt{RNN-ProVe}$), a probabilistic framework that $\textit{estimates the likelihood}$ of undesired behaviors in RNN-based policies. $\texttt{RNN-ProVe}$ uses policy-driven sampling to approximate the set of hidden states that are feasible under a trained policy, and derives statistical error bounds to produce bounded-error, high-confidence estimates of behavioral violations. Experiments on partially observable single-agent and cooperative multi-agent tasks show that $\texttt{RNN-ProVe}$ yields more quantitative, feasibility-aware probabilistic guarantees than existing tools, while scaling to recurrent and multi-agent settings.

Original abstract: MediaClaw is a multimodal agent platform built on the OpenClaw ecosystem. Its core design follows a three-layer architecture of unified abstraction, pluginized extension, and workflow orchestration. The system is intended to address practical deployment pain points in AIGC adoption, including fragmented capabilities, heterogeneous interfaces, disconnected production processes, and limited reuse of high-quality production workflows. \system{} abstracts full-category AIGC capabilities into a unified invocation model, uses plugins to support hot-pluggable capability expansion, and uses task-oriented Skills to turn complex production processes into reusable workflow assets. This report focuses on the architectural design philosophy of MediaClaw, the design logic of its core capability model, and the key engineering trade-offs in implementation. It aims to provide reusable practical reference for building multimodal capability platforms.

### [50] [A Heterogeneous Temporal Memory Governance Framework for Long-Term LLM Persona Consistency](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14802v1)
*Zhao Yang,Wang Huan,Li Yingshuo,Tu Haomiao,Lin Hujite*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 外部时序记忆框架用于长程persona一致性，可迁移至coding agent记忆

TL;DR: 提出ARPM外部时间记忆治理框架，通过分离静态和动态记忆、结合多种检索与排序技术，有效缓解长时对话中的事实丢失、个性漂移等问题，实验证明其可行性与白箱评估性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决大语言模型在长距离交互中面临的事实丢失、时间线混淆、个性漂移及稳定性下降等问题，特别是在高噪声、上下文清除和跨模型迁移场景下。

Method: ARPM框架，将静态知识记忆与动态对话经验记忆分离，结合向量检索、BM25、RRF融合、双时重排序、时间顺序证据阅读及受控分析协议，实现可追踪的连续性治理。

Result: 实验一：不同信噪比下自动召回准确率低于人工审核（如1:5时54.0% vs 100.0%）；实验二：对话历史检索和BM25对精确性关键（严格准确率从100%降至66.7%/80.0%）；实验三：在510万字符噪声、上下文清除和多模型切换下保持连续性，但暴露协议合规性限制。

Conclusion: 长期个性一致性可分解为可治理组件并通过白箱方式评估，ARPM框架提供了有效方案。

中文摘要：大语言模型在长距离交互中经常遭受事实丢失、时间线混淆、个性漂移和稳定性降低的问题，尤其是在高噪声知识库、上下文清除和跨模型迁移的情况下。为了解决这些问题，我们引入了ARPM，一个用于长时对话的外部时间记忆治理框架。ARPM将静态知识记忆与动态对话经验记忆分离，并结合了向量检索、BM25、RRF融合、双时重排序、时间顺序证据阅读以及用于证据验证和答案绑定的受控分析协议。与将个性一致性编码到模型权重中或仅依赖长上下文的方法不同，ARPM将连续性视为一个可追踪、可审计和可转移的治理问题。利用工程日志，我们进行了三个实验。首先，在50轮问答设置中，我们比较了信噪比为1:5和1:200+的情况，并区分了CSV自动判断和人工审核。在1:5下，CSV召回准确率为54.0%，而人工审核将其提升至100.0%。在1:200+下，数值分别为44.0%和80.0%。这些结果表明，当支持性证据进入提示后，自动规则可能会低估召回率。其次，消融结果表明，对话历史检索对于近期连续性来说是必要的：禁用它会将严格准确率从100%降至66.7%，而禁用BM25则降至80.0%，表明纯语义检索不足以进行纠正和追踪。第三，在510万字符的噪声基底、周期性上下文清除和多模型切换下，ARPM保持了语义连续性、边界连续性和个性一致性，同时暴露了由弱协议合规性引起的限制。这些发现表明，长期个性一致性可以分解为可治理的组件，并以白箱方式进行评估。

Original abstract: Large language models often suffer from fact loss, timeline confusion, persona drift, and reduced stability during long-range interaction, especially under high-noise knowledge bases, context clearing, and cross-model transfer. To address these issues, we introduce ARPM, an external temporal memory governance framework for long-term dialogue. ARPM separates static knowledge memory from dynamic dialogue experience memory and combines vector retrieval, BM25, RRF fusion, dual-temporal reranking, chronological evidence reading, and a controlled analysis protocol for evidence verification and answer binding. Unlike approaches that encode persona consistency into model weights or rely only on long context, ARPM treats continuity as a traceable, auditable, and transferable governance problem. Using engineering logs, we conduct three experiments. First, in a 50-round question-answering setting, we compare signal-to-noise ratios of 1:5 and 1:200+, and distinguish CSV auto-judgment from manual review. Under 1:5, CSV recall accuracy is 54.0%, while manual review raises it to 100.0%. Under 1:200+, the values are 44.0% and 80.0%. These results show that automatic rules can underestimate recall after supporting evidence enters the prompt. Second, ablation results show that dialogue history retrieval is necessary for recent continuity: disabling it reduces strict accuracy from 100% to 66.7%, and disabling BM25 reduces it to 80.0%, indicating that pure semantic retrieval is insufficient for correction and tracing. Third, under a 5.1-million-character noise substrate, periodic context clearing, and multi-model handoff, ARPM maintains semantic continuity, boundary continuity, and persona consistency, while exposing limits caused by weak protocol compliance. These findings show that long-term persona consistency can be decomposed into governable components and evaluated in a white-box manner.

### [51] [Interestingness as an Inductive Heuristic for Future Compression Progress](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14831v1)
*Vincent Herrmann,Jürgen Schmidhuber*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 有趣性形式化用于自改进系统，对agent自我改进有理论启发

TL;DR: 形式化有趣性为未来压缩进步的归纳启发式，证明其可预测性，并发现算法先验比长度先验更乐观，预期发现呈二次增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 递归自我改进系统的瓶颈在于识别有潜力的任务或数据，即有趣性。现有方法缺乏形式化定义和可预测性分析。

Method: 基于柯尔莫哥洛夫复杂度和算法统计，分析不同先验下的复杂度-运行时间分布，证明有趣性的归纳性质并推导期望进步公式。

Result: 未来进步期望与最近突破时间呈指数关系；算法先验比长度先验带来二次增长的期望发现；实验验证了三个计算范式。

Conclusion: 有趣性是可形式化且可预测的归纳属性，为递归自我改进系统提供了设计原则，算法先验更具乐观性。

中文摘要：在通往递归自我改进系统的道路上，瓶颈之一是有趣性挑战：即前瞻性地识别哪些任务或数据具有未来进步潜力的能力。我们将有趣性形式化为一种用于未来压缩进步的归纳启发式方法，并利用柯尔莫哥洛夫复杂度和算法统计工具研究其可预测性。通过分析长度先验、算法先验和速度先验下的复杂度-运行时间分布，我们证明了有趣性的归纳特性——即过去进步能够预示未来发现的能力——在理论上是可行的，并且得到了实验支持。我们证明，期望的未来进步取决于最近一次观察到的突破的指数级衰减。此外，我们表明，算法先验比长度先验明显更乐观，对于相同的观测分布，期望发现数量呈二次增长。这些发现在三个不同的通用计算范式上得到了实验证实。

Original abstract: One of the bottlenecks on the way towards recursively self-improving systems is the challenge of interestingness: the ability to prospectively identify which tasks or data hold the potential for future progress. We formalize interestingness as an inductive heuristic for future compression progress and investigate its predictability using tools from Kolmogorov Complexity and Algorithmic Statistics. By analyzing complexity-runtime profiles under Length, Algorithmic, and Speed priors, we demonstrate that the inductive property of interestingness -- the capacity for past progress to signal future discovery -- is theoretically viable and empirically supported. We prove that expected future progress depends exponentially on the recency of the last observed breakthrough. Furthermore, we show that the Algorithmic Prior is significantly more optimistic than the Length Prior, yielding a quadratic increase in expected discovery for the same observed profile. These findings are experimentally confirmed across three diverse universal computational paradigms.

### [52] [Emotion-Attended Stateful Memory (EASM):The Architecture for Hyper-Personalization at Scale](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14833v1)
*Vineet Kotecha,Vansh Gupta*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 记忆增强条件在所有场景中优于基线，记忆基础提升95%，计划清晰度57%，情感验证34%。

Conclusion: 状态情感记忆可能成为超个性化AI系统的基础设施，但需更广泛验证。

中文摘要：当前语言模型系统在会话之间本质上保持无状态，限制了它们随时间进行个性化交互的能力。虽然检索增强生成和微调改进了知识访问和领域能力，但它们无法实现对个体用户的持久理解。我们提出了一种情感注意力状态记忆架构，该架构在推理时使用长期历史、情感信号和推断意图动态构建用户特定的对话上下文。为了评估其影响，我们在两种条件下使用相同的底层语言模型，进行了跨越三十个非脚本对话的受控A/B研究，这些对话涵盖六个情感上不同的类别。记忆增强条件在所有评估场景中均持续优于无状态基线。最大的改进体现在记忆基础（95%）、计划清晰度（57%）和情感验证（34%）方面。即使在涉及悲伤、痛苦和不确定性的情感对抗性对话中，结果也保持一致。这些发现表明，状态情感记忆可能代表超个性化AI系统的基础设施层，但仍有必要在更大规模和更多样化的评估中进行更广泛的验证。

Original abstract: Current language model systems remain fundamentally stateless across sessions, limiting their ability to personalize interactions over time. While retrieval-augmented generation and fine-tuning improve knowledge access and domain capability, they do not enable persistent understanding of individual users. We propose an emotion-attended stateful memory architecture that dynamically constructs user-specific conversational context using long-term history, emotional signals, and inferred intent at inference time. To evaluate its impact, we conducted a controlled A/B study across thirty non-scripted conversations spanning six emotionally distinct categories using the same underlying language model in both conditions. The memory-enriched condition consistently outperformed the stateless baseline across all evaluated scenarios. The largest gains were observed in memory grounding (95% improvement), plan clarity (57%), and emotional validation (34%). Results remained consistent even in emotionally adversarial conversations involving grief, distress, and uncertainty. These findings suggest that stateful emotional memory may represent a foundational infrastructure layer for hyper-personalized AI systems, though broader validation across larger and more diverse evaluations remains necessary

</details>


### [53] [A Deterministic Agentic Workflow for HS Tariff Classification: Multi-Dimensional Rule Reasoning with Interpretable Decisions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14857v1)
*Yu Zhang,Dongjiang Zhuang,Qu Zhou,Zheng Huang,Junhe Wu,Jing Cao,Kai Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 确定性agent工作流用于规则推理，可迁移至coding agent工作流设计

TL;DR: 提出确定性智能工作流解决HS分类多轴规则推理难题，在HSCodeComp上六位top-1达64.2%，并发现数据集标签可能偏离规则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 端到端大模型提示在HS分类中因忽视多轴优先约束而失败，需要可解释且可靠的规则推理方法。

Method: 设计固定控制流的确定性智能工作流，结合离线知识工程与在线六阶段流水线，将LM调用限定于局部阶段，并保留反思与验证机制。

Result: 六位代码top-1 64.2%，top-3 78.3%；开源模型与前沿模型一致性高；人工审核提示数据集标签可能存疑。

Conclusion: 确定性工作流优于端到端方法，提供可解释性，并发现基准数据集可能需修正。

中文摘要：协调制度（HS）关税分类是一项高风险、专家级的任务，需要将自由形式的产品描述映射到通用解释规则（GIR）、类注、章注和解释说明下的特定六位或八位代码。其难点不在于知识量，而在于*多维度规则推理*：正确的分类必须同时满足几个轴上的竞争性优先规则，包括材料、形状、功能、基本特征、部分与整体的界限，以及具体列名与剩余税目。大型语言模型的端到端提示在典型情况下会失败，因为它只解决了一个轴而忽略了其他轴上的优先约束。我们提出了一种*确定性智能工作流*，与自规划智能体形成对比：控制流是固定的，语言模型调用被限制在狭窄的阶段，反思和验证作为局部机制保留。这种设计通过构造实现了可解释性——每个决策被分解为阶段性的结构化输出，并逐字引用与之相关的章注或类注。该架构将中国HS关税的离线知识工程与在线六阶段流水线相结合。在HSCodeComp数据集上以六位代码水平评估，该工作流在使用Qwen3.6-plus时，四位代码达到75.0%的top-1和91.5%的top-3，六位代码达到64.2%的top-1和78.3%的top-3；使用非思考模式下的开源Qwen3.6-27B-FP8骨干网络，与前沿模型在四位代码上达到84.2%的一致性，六位代码上达到77.4%的top-1一致性。对226个六位代码不一致项进行的两阶段人工审核表明，HSCodeComp真实标签中有相当一部分可能与HS通用规则存在偏差；完整的判定记录作为初步发现发布在附录中，供社区审查。

Original abstract: Harmonized System (HS) tariff classification is a high-stakes, expert-level task in which a free-form product description must be mapped to a specific six- or eight-digit code under the General Interpretive Rules (GIR), section notes, chapter notes, and Explanatory Notes. The difficulty lies not in knowledge volume but in *multi-dimensional rule reasoning*: a correct classification must satisfy competing priority rules along several axes simultaneously, including material, form, function, essential character, the part-versus-whole boundary, and specific listing versus residual headings. End-to-end prompting of large language models fails characteristically by resolving one axis while ignoring the priority constraints on the others. We present a *deterministic agentic workflow* in contrast to self-planning agents: the control flow is fixed, language model calls are confined to narrow stages, and reflection and verification are retained as local mechanisms. This design yields interpretability by construction--each decision is decomposed into stage-wise structured outputs with verbatim citation of the chapter or section notes that bear on it. The architecture combines offline knowledge-engineering of the Chinese HS tariff with an online six-stage pipeline. Evaluated on HSCodeComp at the six-digit level, the workflow reaches 75.0% top-1 and 91.5% top-3 at four digits, and 64.2% top-1 and 78.3% top-3 at six digits with Qwen3.6-plus; an open-weight Qwen3.6-27B-FP8 backbone in non-thinking mode achieves 84.2% four-digit and 77.4% six-digit top-1 agreement with the frontier model. A two-stage manual audit of 226 six-digit disagreements suggests that a non-trivial fraction of HSCodeComp ground-truth labels may deviate from HS general rules; full adjudication records are released in the appendix as preliminary findings for community review.

</details>


### [54] [Holistic Evaluation and Failure Diagnosis of AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14865v1)
*Netta Madvil,Gilad Dym,Alon Mecilati,Edo Dekel,Jonatan Liberman,Rotem Brazilay,Liron Schliesser,Max Svidlo,Shai Nir,Orel Shalom,Yaron Friedman,David Connack,Amos Rimon,Philip Tannor,Shir Chorev*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出agent评估与失败诊断框架，在SWE-Bench等benchmark上验证，直接相关agent方法论。

TL;DR: 提出一个结合自上而下和自下而上评估的代理评估框架，在TRAIL基准上显著优于现有方法，揭示了评估方法论而非模型能力是瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估要么只报告结果成功/失败，要么难以定位失败类型在长轨迹中的位置。

Method: 提出整体框架，结合自上而下代理级诊断与自下而上跨度级评估，将分析分解为独立每个跨度评估。

Result: 在TRAIL上所有指标最先进，类别F1提升38%，定位准确率提升3.5倍，联合准确率提升12.5倍；相同模型在框架内定位准确率高数倍。

Conclusion: 评估方法论是瓶颈，框架证明了分解评估的有效性。

中文摘要：AI代理执行复杂的多步骤过程，但当前的评估存在不足：结果指标报告成功或失败，而不解释原因；过程级方法难以将失败类型与其在长结构化轨迹中的精确位置联系起来。我们提出了一个整体的代理评估框架，它将自上而下的代理级诊断与自下而上的跨度级评估相结合，将分析分解为独立的每个跨度评估。这种分解可扩展到任意长度的轨迹，并为每个判定产生跨度级理由。在TRAIL基准测试中，我们的框架在GAIA和SWE-Bench上的所有指标上均取得了最先进的结果，相较于之前最强的基线，在类别F1上相对提升高达38%，在定位准确率上高达3.5倍，在联合定位-分类准确率上高达12.5倍。按类别分析显示，我们的框架在更多错误类别中领先于任何其他评估器。值得注意的是，相同的前沿模型在我们框架内使用时，其定位准确率比作为整体评判器对整个轨迹进行评判时高出数倍，这表明评估方法，而非模型能力，才是瓶颈。

Original abstract: AI agents execute complex multi-step processes, but current evaluation falls short: outcome metrics report success or failure without explaining why, and process-level approaches struggle to connect failure types to their precise locations within long, structured traces. We present a holistic agent evaluation framework that pairs top-down agent-level diagnosis with bottom-up span-level evaluation, decomposing analysis into independent per-span assessments. This decomposition scales to traces of arbitrary length and produces span-level rationales for each verdict. On the TRAIL benchmark, our framework achieves state-of-the-art results across all metrics on both GAIA and SWE-Bench, with relative gains over the strongest prior baselines of up to 38% on category F1, up to 3.5x on localization accuracy, and up to 12.5x on joint localization-categorization accuracy. Per-category analysis shows our framework leading in more error categories than any other evaluator. Notably, the same frontier model achieves several times higher localization accuracy when used inside our framework than as a monolithic judge over the full trace, showing that evaluation methodology, not model capability, is the bottleneck.

### [55] [Beyond Individual Intelligence: Surveying Collaboration, Failure Attribution, and Self-Evolution in LLM-based Multi-Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14892v2)
*Shihao Qi,Jie Ma,Rui Xing,Wei Guo,Xiao Huang,Zhitao Gao,Jianhao Deng,Jun Liu,Lingling Zhang,Bifan Wei,Boqian Yang,Pinghui Wang,Jianwen Sun,Jing Tao,Yaqiang Wu,Hui Liu,Yu Yao,Tongliang Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent系统综述，涵盖协作、失败归因与自我进化，对agent架构设计有直接指导意义。

TL;DR: 本文提出LIFE框架，统一了多智能体系统从能力构建到自我演化的四个阶段，并指出了跨阶段的研究挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有调查分别覆盖个体智能体能力、多智能体协作和智能体自我演化，未考察它们之间的因果依赖关系，导致错误传播和诊断困难等问题未被系统性研究。

Method: 通过提出LIFE框架（奠定能力基础、整合智能体、归因故障、自主进化），对每个阶段进行系统分类，并形式化描述相邻阶段间的依赖关系，识别阶段边界挑战，提出跨阶段研究议程。

Result: 提供了一个统一综述，揭示了多智能体系统各阶段间的因果依赖，识别了边界处的开放挑战，并提出了面向闭环自改进系统的研究方向。

Conclusion: 本调查旨在为自主、自我改进的多智能体系统提供系统性参考和概念性路线图，推动从当前协调框架向更自组织的集体智能演进。

中文摘要：基于LLM的自主智能体在推理、规划和工具使用方面展现出了强大的能力，但当任务需要跨角色、工具和环境的持续协调时，它们仍然存在局限性。多智能体系统通过专业智能体之间的结构化协作来解决这一问题，但更紧密的协调也放大了较少被探索的风险：错误可以在智能体和交互轮次之间传播，产生难以诊断的失败，并且很少转化为结构性的自我改进。现有调查分别涵盖了个体智能体能力、多智能体协作或智能体自我演化，未考察它们之间的因果依赖关系。本调查提供了一个统一综述，围绕四个因果关联的阶段组织，我们称之为LIFE演进：奠定能力基础、通过协作整合智能体、通过归因发现故障、通过自主自我改进进化。对于每个阶段，我们提供了系统化的分类法，并正式描述了相邻阶段之间的依赖关系，揭示了每个阶段如何依赖并约束下一个阶段。除了综合现有工作，我们识别了阶段边界处的开放挑战，并提出了一个跨阶段的研究议程，用于能够持续诊断故障、重组结构和优化智能体行为的闭环多智能体系统，将当前的协调框架扩展到更自组织的集体智能形式。通过连接这些先前碎片化的研究线索，本调查旨在提供系统性的参考和概念性路线图，以实现自主、自我改进的多智能体智能。

Original abstract: LLM-based autonomous agents have demonstrated strong capabilities in reasoning, planning, and tool use, yet remain limited when tasks require sustained coordination across roles, tools, and environments. Multi-agent systems address this through structured collaboration among specialized agents, but tighter coordination also amplifies a less explored risk: errors can propagate across agents and interaction rounds, producing failures that are difficult to diagnose and rarely translate into structural self-improvement. Existing surveys cover individual agent capabilities, multi-agent collaboration, or agent self-evolution separately, leaving the causal dependencies among them unexamined. This survey provides a unified review organized around four causally linked stages, which we term the LIFE progression: Lay the capability foundation, Integrate agents through collaboration, Find faults through attribution, and Evolve through autonomous self-improvement. For each stage, we provide systematic taxonomies and formally characterize the dependencies between adjacent stages, revealing how each stage both depends on and constrains the next. Beyond synthesizing existing work, we identify open challenges at stage boundaries and propose a cross-stage research agenda for closed-loop multi-agent systems capable of continuously diagnosing failures, reorganizing structures, and refining agent behaviors, extending current coordination frameworks toward more self-organizing forms of collective intelligence. By bridging these previously fragmented research threads, this survey aims to offer both a systematic reference and a conceptual roadmap toward autonomous, self-improving multi-agent intelligence.

### [56] [GraphFlow: An Architecture for Formally Verifiable Visual Workflows Enabling Reliable Agentic AI Automation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14968v1)
*Drewry H. Morris,Luis Valles,Reza Hosseini Ghomi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出验证可靠的工作流架构用于agent自动化，对构建可靠的软件工程agent有参考价值。

TL;DR: GraphFlow通过将工作流图作为可执行规范，结合编译时契约证明检查和运行时持久化引擎，提高了多步骤AI自动化流程的可靠性。试点实验显示97.08%的完成率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作流平台缺乏语义正确性保证，且智能体系统行为对提示敏感、难以审计，导致多步骤关键任务中错误累积严重。

Method: 将工作流图视为可执行规范，定义数据范围、执行语义和监控；编译时对受限图类生成可复用自动化，契约需经证明检查；运行时使用持久化引擎记录事件日志，系统边界强制执行契约，泳道明确信任边界。

Result: 三年临床站点试点，8,728次运行，97.08%完成率，失败主要来自外部集成。

Conclusion: GraphFlow的正式语义和证明检查模型已在开发中，验证核心的评估留待未来工作。

中文摘要：GraphFlow是一个可视化工作流系统，旨在提高多步骤、关键任务场景中基于智能体的AI自动化的可靠性。在这些工作流中，小错误会迅速累积：在一个独立的理想化步骤模型中，如果每一步的可靠性为90%，一个十步流程的成功完成率仅为35%。现有的工作流平台提供持久化执行和可观测性，但缺乏语义正确性保证，而基于智能体的系统在推理时进行规划，导致行为对提示变化敏感且难以审计。GraphFlow旨在通过将工作流图视为可执行规范来填补这一空白，这是一个定义数据范围、执行语义和监控的单一工件。在编译时，指定一个受限的图类以生成可复用的自动化，其契约（前置条件、后置条件和组合义务）旨在被纳入共享库之前进行证明检查。在运行时，一个持久化引擎将结果记录在仅追加的事件日志中，并可以在系统边界强制执行契约，支持重放、重试和审计。泳道使信任边界明确，将经过验证的逻辑与外部系统、人类判断和AI决策分离开来。一项在三个临床站点进行的为期一年的试点测试执行了8,728次队列入组工作流运行，在早期原型（不含经过验证的核心子系统）下完成了97.08%；观察到的失败主要局限于外部集成。这里描述的正式语义和经过证明检查的准入模型已被指定并正在积极开发中。对经过验证的核心的评估留给未来的工作。

Original abstract: GraphFlow is a visual workflow system designed to improve the reliability of agentic AI automation in multi-step, mission-critical processes. In these workflows, small errors compound rapidly: under an idealized model of independent steps, a ten-step process with 90% per-step reliability completes successfully only 35% of the time. Existing workflow platforms provide durable execution and observability but offer few semantic correctness guarantees, while agentic systems plan at inference time, making behavior sensitive to prompt variation and difficult to audit.
  GraphFlow is designed to address this gap by treating workflow diagrams as the executable specification, a single artifact defining data scope, execution semantics, and monitoring. At compile time, a restricted class of diagrams is specified to produce reusable automations whose contracts (preconditions, postconditions, and composition obligations) are intended to be proof-checked before admission to a shared library. At runtime, a durable engine records outcomes in an append-only event log and can enforce contracts at system boundaries, supporting replay, retries, and audit. Swimlanes make trust boundaries explicit, separating verified logic from external systems, human judgment, and AI decisions.
  A year-long pilot across three clinical sites executed 8,728 cohort-enrolled workflow runs with a 97.08% completion rate under an early prototype without the verified-core subsystem; observed failures were localized primarily to external integrations. The formal semantics and proof-checked admission model described here are specified and under active development. Evaluation of the verified core is reserved for future work.

</details>


### [57] [Orchard: An Open-Source Agentic Modeling Framework](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15040v2)
*Baolin Peng,Wenlin Yao,Qianhui Wu,Hao Cheng,Xiao Yu,Rui Yang,Tao Ge,Alessandro Sordoni,Xingdi Yuan,Yelong Shen,Pengcheng He,Tong Zhang,Zhou Yu,Jianfeng Gao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 开源agent建模框架，涵盖coding agent训练与评估

TL;DR: Orchard是一个开源框架，通过轻量级环境服务Orchard Env实现可扩展的代理建模，在编码、GUI和助理代理任务上取得SOTA或竞争力强的结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有开放研究受限于基础设施和训练差距，高性能系统依赖专有组件，开源框架缺乏可扩展的代理训练支持。

Method: 提出Orchard框架，核心为Orchard Env环境服务；针对三个领域构建方案：Orchard-SWE（蒸馏+信用分配SFT+平衡自适应RL）、Orchard-GUI（少量蒸馏轨迹+开放式任务训练）、Orchard-Claw（少量合成任务训练）。

Result: Orchard-SWE在SWE-bench Verified上达到67.5%；Orchard-GUI在WebVoyager等上达到74.1%成功率；Orchard-Claw在Claw-Eval上达到59.6% pass@3。

Conclusion: 轻量级、开放、工具无关的环境层能够跨领域实现可重用的代理数据、训练方案和评估，推动开源代理研究。

中文摘要：Agentic建模旨在将LLM转变为能够通过规划、推理、工具使用以及与环境的多轮交互来解决复杂任务的自主代理。尽管有大量投入，但开放研究仍然受到基础设施和训练差距的限制。许多高性能系统依赖于专有代码库、模型或服务，而大多数开源框架侧重于编排和评估，而不是可扩展的代理训练。我们提出了Orchard，一个用于可扩展代理建模的开源框架。其核心是Orchard Env，一个轻量级环境服务，为任务领域、代理工具和流水线阶段提供可重用的沙箱生命周期管理原语。在Orchard Env之上，我们构建了三个代理建模方案。Orchard-SWE针对编码代理。我们从MiniMax-M2.5和Qwen3.5-397B中蒸馏了107K条轨迹，引入了信用分配SFT来从未解决轨迹的产出片段中学习，并应用平衡自适应 rollout 进行RL。从Qwen3-30B-A3B-Thinking开始，Orchard-SWE在SWE-bench Verified上经过SFT后达到64.3%，经过SFT+RL后达到67.5%，在类似规模的开源模型中创造了新的最先进水平。Orchard-GUI仅使用0.4K蒸馏轨迹和2.2K开放任务训练了一个4B视觉语言计算机使用代理。它在WebVoyager、Online-Mind2Web和DeepShop上分别达到74.1%、67.0%和64.0%的成功率，成为最强的开源模型，同时与专有系统保持竞争力。Orchard-Claw针对个人助理代理。仅用0.2K合成任务训练，它在Claw-Eval上达到59.6%的pass@3，当与更强的ZeroClaw工具配合时达到73.9%。总体而言，这些结果表明，轻量级、开放、工具无关的环境层能够在不同领域实现可重用的代理数据、训练方案和评估。

Original abstract: Agentic modeling aims to transform LLMs into autonomous agents capable of solving complex tasks through planning, reasoning, tool use, and multi-turn interaction with environments. Despite major investment, open research remains constrained by infrastructure and training gaps. Many high-performing systems rely on proprietary codebases, models, or services, while most open-source frameworks focus on orchestration and evaluation rather than scalable agent training. We present Orchard, an open-source framework for scalable agentic modeling. At its core is Orchard Env, a lightweight environment service providing reusable primitives for sandbox lifecycle management across task domains, agent harnesses, and pipeline stages. On top of Orchard Env, we build three agentic modeling recipes. Orchard-SWE targets coding agents. We distill 107K trajectories from MiniMax-M2.5 and Qwen3.5-397B, introduce credit-assignment SFT to learn from productive segments of unresolved trajectories, and apply Balanced Adaptive Rollout for RL. Starting from Qwen3-30B-A3B-Thinking, Orchard-SWE achieves 64.3% on SWE-bench Verified after SFT and 67.5% after SFT+RL, setting a new state of the art among open-source models of comparable size. Orchard-GUI trains a 4B vision-language computer-use agent using only 0.4K distilled trajectories and 2.2K open-ended tasks. It achieves 74.1%, 67.0%, and 64.0% success rates on WebVoyager, Online-Mind2Web, and DeepShop, respectively, making it the strongest open-source model while remaining competitive with proprietary systems. Orchard-Claw targets personal assistant agents. Trained with only 0.2K synthetic tasks, it achieves 59.6% pass@3 on Claw-Eval and 73.9% when paired with a stronger ZeroClaw harness. Collectively, these results show that a lightweight, open, harness-agnostic environment layer enables reusable agentic data, training recipes, and evaluations across domains.

### [58] [Case-Based Calibration of Adaptive Reasoning and Execution for LLM Tool Use](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15041v1)
*Renning Pang,Tian Lan,Leyuan Liu,Piao Tong,Sheng Cao,Xiaosong Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 案例驱动工具使用agent，优化推理与结构有效性

TL;DR: CAST是一个案例驱动的框架，通过提取历史执行轨迹中的复杂度与失败信号指导推理深度和结构有效性，在工具使用任务中提升准确率并减少推理长度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

中文摘要：工具使用将大型语言模型扩展到参数化知识之外，但可靠的执行需要在适当的推理深度和严格的结构有效性之间取得平衡。我们从基于案例的角度处理这个问题，提出了CAST，一个案例驱动的框架，将历史执行轨迹视为结构化案例。CAST不是重复使用原始示例输出，而是提取案例派生信号来识别复杂度概况以估计最优推理策略，以及失败概况以映射可能的结构性故障。该框架将这些知识转化为细粒度的奖励设计和自适应推理，使模型能够在强化学习过程中自主内化基于案例的策略。在BFCLv2和ToolBench上的实验表明，CAST既提高了模式忠实执行和任务级工具使用成功率，又减少了不必要的推理。该方法在整体执行准确性上实现了高达5.85个百分点的提升，并将平均推理长度减少了26%，显著减轻了高影响的结构性错误。最终，这证明了历史执行案例如何为校准的工具使用提供可复用的适应知识。

Original abstract: Tool use extends large language models beyond parametric knowledge, but reliable execution requires balancing appropriate reasoning depth with strict structural validity. We approach this problem from a case-based perspective to present CAST, a case-driven framework that treats historical execution trajectories as structured cases. Instead of reusing raw exemplar outputs, CAST extracts case-derived signals to identify complexity profiles for estimating optimal reasoning strategies, alongside failure profiles to map likely structural breakdowns. The framework translates this knowledge into a fine-grained reward design and adaptive reasoning, enabling the model to autonomously internalize case-based strategies during reinforcement learning. Experiments on BFCLv2 and ToolBench demonstrate that CAST improves both schema-faithful execution and task-level tool-use success while reducing unnecessary deliberation. The approach achieves up to 5.85 percentage points gain in overall execution accuracy and reduces average reasoning length by 26%, significantly mitigating high-impact structural errors. Ultimately, this demonstrates how historical execution cases can provide reusable adaptation knowledge for calibrated tool use.

### [59] [Dual-Dimensional Consistency: Balancing Budget and Quality in Adaptive Inference-Time Scaling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15100v1)
*Rongman Xu,Yifei Li,Tianzhe Zhao,Yanrui Wu,Bo Li,Hang Yan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 推理时自适应缩放，通用LLM推理优化可迁移至agent

TL;DR: DDC通过将置信度加权贝叶斯协议与趋势感知剪枝相结合，实现自适应推理深度，在保持准确率的同时将令牌消耗降低10倍以上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前推理时缩放方法将采样宽度和深度视为正交目标，宽度方法易强化幻觉，深度方法过早截断有效链，缺乏统一框架来平衡质量和效率。

Method: DDC耦合置信度加权贝叶斯协议评估路径质量，并结合趋势感知分层剪枝自适应终止低质量路径，将计算资源集中在高质量推理上。

Result: 在五个基准上，DDC将令牌消耗减少10倍以上，同时保持或超过多种LLM上强基线的准确率。

Conclusion: DDC为推理时缩放提供了高效框架，有效平衡了推理质量和计算成本。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）在推理方面表现出了卓越的能力。然而，通过推理时缩放来最大化其潜力面临着采样预算和推理质量之间的权衡挑战。当前的策略仍然效率低下，因为它们通常将采样宽度和深度视为正交目标，其中宽度共识方法有强化幻觉的风险，而深度剪枝机制过早地截断复杂但有效的推理链。因此，我们提出了双维一致性（DDC），这是一个统一框架，将路径质量与自适应终止联系起来。通过将置信度加权贝叶斯协议与趋势感知分层剪枝相结合，我们的方法确保计算资源集中在高质量推理路径上，过滤幻觉同时加速共识。在五个基准上的评估表明，该方法将令牌消耗减少了10倍以上，同时保持或超过了各种LLM上的强基线的准确性。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable abilities in reasoning. However, maximizing their potential through inference-time scaling faces challenges in trade-off between sampling budget and reasoning quality. Current strategies remain inefficient as they typically treat sampling width and depth as orthogonal objectives, where width consensus methods risk reinforcing hallucinations, while depth pruning mechanisms prematurely truncate complex yet valid reasoning chains. Therefore, we propose Dual-Dimensional Consistency (DDC), a unified framework that bridges path quality with adaptive termination. By coupling Confidence-Weighted Bayesian protocol with a Trend-Aware Stratified Pruning, our method ensures that computational resources are concentrated on high quality reasoning paths, filtering hallucinations while accelerating consensus. Evaluations across five benchmarks demonstrate that this approach reduces token consumption by over 10 times while maintaining or exceeding the accuracy of strong baselines across various LLMs.

### [60] [Why Neighborhoods Matter: Traversal Context and Provenance in Agentic GraphRAG](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15109v1)
*Riccardo Terrenzi,Maximilian von Zastrow,Serkan Ayvaz*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: Agentic GraphRAG中引用忠实性研究，涉及agent轨迹分析

TL;DR: 代理型图检索增强生成中，引用忠实性不仅需要答案支持证据，还需考虑图谱遍历和未引用实体；消融实验表明引用必要但不充分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的引用评估仅关注答案与引用证据的支持关系，忽略了代理型图检索增强生成中图谱遍历和未引用实体的影响。

Method: 通过受控消融实验，隔离、移除和掩盖已引用和未引用图实体，观察对答案的影响。

Result: 被引用的证据是必要的（移除后答案改变、准确性降低），但引用不充分（准确答案依赖于未引用的遍历上下文和图结构）。

Conclusion: 代理型图检索增强生成中的引用评估应超越源支持，转向对更广泛检索轨迹的溯源。

中文摘要：检索增强生成可以通过将答案基于外部证据来提高事实准确性，但代理型图检索增强生成（Agentic GraphRAG）使引用的忠实性变得复杂。在这些系统中，代理在生成答案和少量引用之前会探索知识图谱。我们将引用忠实性定义为一个轨迹级问题：最终引用不仅应支持答案，还应考虑图谱遍历、结构以及可能影响答案的已访问但未引用的实体。通过受控消融实验，我们比较了隔离、移除和掩盖已引用和未引用图实体的效果。我们的结果表明，被引用的证据通常是必要的，因为移除它会显著改变答案并降低准确性。然而，引用并不充分，因为准确的答案也可能依赖于未引用的遍历上下文和周围的图结构。这些发现表明，代理型图检索增强生成中的引用评估应超越源支持，转向更广泛的检索轨迹的溯源。

Original abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation can improve factuality by grounding answers in external evidence, but Agentic GraphRAG complicates what it means for citations to be faithful. In these systems, an agent explores a knowledge graph before producing an answer and a small set of citations. We frame citation faithfulness as a trajectory-level problem: final citations should not only support the answer, but also account for the graph traversal, structure, and visited-but-uncited entities that may influence it. Through controlled ablation experiments, we compare the effects of isolating, removing, and masking cited and uncited graph entities. Our results show that cited evidence is often necessary, as removing it substantially changes answers and reduces accuracy. However, citations are not sufficient, because accurate answers can also depend on uncited traversal context and surrounding graph structure. These findings suggest that citation evaluation in Agentic GraphRAG should move beyond source support toward provenance over the broader retrieval trajectory.

### [61] [APWA: A Distributed Architecture for Parallelizable Agentic Workflows](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15132v1)
*Evan Rose,Tushin Mallick,Matthew D. Laws,Cristina Nita-Rotaru,Alina Oprea*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 分布式多agent工作流架构，直接提升agent可扩展性

TL;DR: 提出一种分布式多智能体系统架构APWA，通过将工作流分解为非干扰子问题并并行处理，解决了大规模复杂任务中的扩展瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的多智能体系统在处理大规模复杂任务时面临推理、协调和计算扩展瓶颈，无法有效利用并行资源。

Method: APWA通过将工作流分解为无需跨通信的非干扰子问题，使用独立资源并行处理，支持异构数据和多种并行模式。

Result: APWA能够动态分解复杂查询为可并行化工作流，在更大任务上成功扩展，而先前系统完全失败。

Conclusion: APWA是一种有效的架构，能够高效处理高度可并行化的智能体工作负载，克服现有系统的扩展限制。

中文摘要：基于大语言模型（LLM）的自主多智能体系统在广泛应用领域内独立解决复杂任务方面展现出了卓越的能力。然而，随着任务规模和复杂性的增长，这些系统在推理、协调和计算扩展方面遇到了关键瓶颈。尽管底层LLM中存在并行计算和推理原语，但这些限制阻碍了多智能体系统实现对高度可并行化任务的高吞吐量处理。我们引入了智能体并行工作负载架构（APWA），这是一种分布式多智能体系统架构，专为高效处理高度可并行化的智能体工作负载而设计。APWA通过将工作流分解为无需跨通信即可使用独立资源处理的非干扰子问题来促进并行执行。它支持异构数据和并行处理模式，并适应广泛领域的任务。在我们的评估中，我们证明了APWA能够将复杂查询动态分解为可并行化的工作流，并在先前系统完全失败的更大任务上实现扩展。

Original abstract: Autonomous multi-agent systems based on large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable abilities in independently solving complex tasks in a wide breadth of application domains. However, these systems hit critical reasoning, coordination, and computational scaling bottlenecks as the size and complexity of their tasks grow. These limitations hinder multi-agent systems from achieving high-throughput processing for highly parallelizable tasks, despite the availability of parallel computing and reasoning primitives in the underlying LLMs. We introduce the Agent-Parallel Workload Architecture (APWA), a distributed multi-agent system architecture designed for the efficient processing of heavily parallelizable agentic workloads. APWA facilitates parallel execution by decomposing workflows into non-interfering subproblems that can be processed using independent resources without cross-communication. It supports heterogeneous data and parallel processing patterns, and it accommodates tasks from a wide breadth of domains. In our evaluation, we demonstrate that APWA can dynamically decompose complex queries into parallelizable workflows and scales on larger tasks in settings where prior systems fail completely.

### [62] [OpenDeepThink: Parallel Reasoning via Bradley-Terry Aggregation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15177v2)
*Shang Zhou,Wenhao Chai,Kaiyuan Liu,Huanzhi Mao,Qiuyang Mang,Jingbo Shang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出并行推理与Bradley-Terry选择框架，可迁移至coding agent的候选方案选择。

TL;DR: 提出OpenDeepThink框架，通过成对Bradley-Terry比较选择候选，显著提升LLM推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法扩展深度但广度引入选择瓶颈，点状LLM判断有噪声和偏差。

Method: 基于种群的测试时计算框架：每代随机配对候选进行LLM判断，通过Bradley-Terry聚合投票为全局排名，保留高排名候选并变异前四分之三，丢弃后四分之一。

Result: OpenDeepThink在八轮LLM调用中使Gemini 3.1 Pro的Codeforces Elo提升+405；可跨模型迁移；在客观域增益明显，主观域逆转。

Conclusion: OpenDeepThink有效提升测试时推理性能，并发布CF-73数据集。

中文摘要：测试时计算扩展是提升LLM推理的主要方向。现有方法主要通过在单个推理链上增加深度来扩展。通过并行采样多个候选来扩展广度是直接的，但引入了一个选择瓶颈：在没有真实验证器的情况下选择最佳候选，因为逐点LLM判断存在噪声和偏差。为解决此问题，我们提出了OpenDeepThink，一种基于种群的测试时计算框架，通过成对Bradley-Terry比较进行选择。每一代，LLM判断随机配对的候选，并通过Bradley-Terry将投票聚合为全局排名；保留排名靠前的候选，并对前四分之三使用比较过程中产生的自然语言批评进行变异；丢弃后四分之一。OpenDeepThink在八个顺序LLM调用轮次（约27分钟挂钟时间）内将Gemini 3.1 Pro的有效Codeforces Elo提高了+405分。该流程可跨不同强度的模型迁移而无需重新调整，在多领域HLE基准测试中，增益集中在客观可验证的领域，而在主观领域则出现逆转。我们发布了CF-73，一组由专家评分的73个Codeforces问题，具有国际特级大师注释，与官方裁决的本地评估一致性达99%。

Original abstract: Test-time compute scaling is a primary axis for improving LLM reasoning. Existing methods primarily scale depth by extending a single reasoning trace. Scaling breadth by sampling multiple candidates in parallel is straightforward, but introduces a selection bottleneck: choosing the best candidate without a ground-truth verifier, since pointwise LLM judging is noisy and biased. To address this, we introduce OpenDeepThink, a population-based test-time compute framework that selects via pairwise Bradley-Terry comparison. Each generation, the LLM judges random pairs of candidates and aggregates votes via Bradley-Terry into a global ranking; top-ranked candidates are preserved and the top three quarters are mutated using the natural-language critiques produced during comparison; the bottom quarter is discarded. OpenDeepThink raises Gemini 3.1 Pro's effective Codeforces Elo by +405 points in eight sequential LLM-call rounds (~27 minutes wall-clock). The pipeline transfers across weaker and stronger models without retuning, and on the multi-domain HLE benchmark, gains appear concentrated in objectively verifiable domains and reverse in subjective ones. We release CF-73, a curated set of 73 expert-rated Codeforces problems with International Grandmaster annotation and 99% local-evaluation agreement against the official verdict.

</details>


### [63] [Solvita: Enhancing Large Language Models for Competitive Programming via Agentic Evolution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15301v1)
*Han Li,Jinyu Tian,Rili Feng,Yuqiao Du,Chong Zheng,Chenyu Wang,Chenchen Liu,Shihao Li,Xinping Lei,Yifan Yao,Weihao Xie,Letian Zhu,Jiaheng Liu*
