<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM多智能体框架无状态，无法积累过去的推理经验，限制其在复杂编程问题上的表现。

Method: 提出Solvita，包含四个智能体（Planner, Solver, Oracle, Hacker），每个配有可训练的图知识网络，利用强化学习从结果信号中更新网络权重，实现持续学习。

Result: 在CodeContests、APPS、AetherCode和实时Codeforces上达到新SOTA，优于现有方法，准确率接近单次基线两倍。

Conclusion: Solvita通过动态知识积累有效提升LLM在竞争性编程中的推理能力，无需更新模型权重。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）在高难度竞争性编程的严格推理要求上仍然存在困难。虽然最近的多智能体框架试图弥合这一可靠性差距，但它们基本上是无状态的：它们依赖静态检索，并丢弃了从先前任务中获得的有价值的解决问题的调试经验。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了Solvita，一个无需更新底层LLM权重即可实现持续学习的智能体进化框架。Solvita将问题解决重新组织为一个闭环系统，包括策略选择、程序合成、认证监督和定向攻击，由四个专门智能体执行：规划者（Planner）、求解者（Solver）、预言者（Oracle）和黑客（Hacker）。关键是，每个智能体都与一个可训练的图结构知识网络配对。随着系统运行，结果信号，例如通过/失败判定、测试认证质量以及黑客发现的对抗性漏洞，被转化为对这些网络权重的强化学习更新。这使得智能体能够根据过去的成功和失败动态路由未来的查询，从而有效地积累可迁移的推理经验。在CodeContests、APPS、AetherCode和实时Codeforces轮次上的评估表明，Solvita在代码生成智能体中建立了新的最先进水平，优于现有的多智能体流水线，并且几乎将单次通过基线的准确性提高了一倍。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) still struggle with the rigorous reasoning demands of hard competitive programming. While recent multi-agent frameworks attempt to bridge this reliability gap, they remain fundamentally stateless: they rely on static retrieval and discard the valuable problem-solving and debugging experience gained from previous tasks. To address this, we present Solvita, an agentic evolution framework that enables continuous learning without requiring weight updates to the underlying LLM. Solvita reorganizes problem-solving into a closed-loop system of strategy selection, program synthesis, certified supervision, and targeted hacking, executed by four specialized agents: Planner, Solver, Oracle, and Hacker. Crucially, each agent is paired with a trainable, graph-structured knowledge network. As the system operates, outcome signals, such as pass/fail verdicts, test certification quality, and adversarial vulnerabilities discovered by the Hacker, are recast as reinforcement learning updates to these network weights. This allows the agents to dynamically route future queries based on past successes and failures, effectively accumulating transferable reasoning experience over time. Evaluated across CodeContests, APPS, AetherCode, and live Codeforces rounds, Solvita establishes a new state-of-the-art among code-generation agents, outperforming existing multi-agent pipelines and nearly doubling the accuracy of single-pass baselines.

</details>


### [64] [SMCEvolve: Principled Scientific Discovery via Sequential Monte Carlo Evolution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15308v1)
*Jiachen Jiang,Huminhao Zhu,Zhihui Zhu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 基于SMC的LLM驱动程序进化，提供收敛保证，直接适用于自动代码优化与科学发现。

TL;DR: SMCEvolve通过顺序蒙特卡洛将程序搜索转化为采样问题，利用三个原则性组件和复杂度分析，在多个基准上以更少LLM调用超越最先进系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM驱动的程序演化框架缺乏设计原则且不保证收敛，需要更可靠、有理论依据的方法。

Method: 将程序搜索建模为从奖励倾斜分布采样，用顺序蒙特卡洛（SMC）近似，包含自适应父代重采样、混合变异与接受、自动收敛控制，并提供有限样本复杂度分析。

Result: 在数学、算法效率、符号回归和端到端机器学习研究基准上，SMCEvolve以更少LLM调用超越最先进的进化系统。

Conclusion: SMCEvolve提供了一种有原则且高效的LLM驱动程序演化方法，具有收敛保证和实际优越性。

中文摘要：LLM驱动的程序演化已成为自动化科学发现的强大工具，然而现有框架在设计其各个组件时缺乏原则性指导，且无法保证搜索收敛。我们提出了SMCEvolve，它将程序搜索重新定义为从奖励倾斜的目标分布中采样，并使用顺序蒙特卡洛（SMC）采样器来近似。从这个视角出发，三个核心机制作为有原则的组件出现：自适应父代重采样、混合变异与接受、自动收敛控制。我们进一步提供了有限样本复杂度分析，限定了达到目标近似误差所需的LLM调用预算。在数学、算法效率、符号回归和端到端机器学习研究基准测试中，SMCEvolve在自我决定的终止条件下使用更少的LLM调用超越了最先进的进化系统。代码可在https://github.com/kongwanbianjinyu/SMCEvolve获取。

Original abstract: LLM-driven program evolution has emerged as a powerful tool for automated scientific discovery, yet existing frameworks offer no principled guide for designing their individual components and provide no guarantee that the search converges. We introduce SMCEvolve, which recasts program search as sampling from a reward-tilted target distribution and approximates it with a Sequential Monte Carlo (SMC) sampler. From this view, three core mechanisms emerge as principled components: adaptive parent resampling, mixture of mutation with acceptance, and automatic convergence control. We further provide a finite-sample complexity analysis that bounds the LLM-call budget required to reach a target approximation error. Across math, algorithm efficiency, symbolic regression, and end-to-end ML research benchmarks, SMCEvolve surpasses state-of-the-art evolving systems while using fewer LLM calls under self-determined termination. The code is available at https://github.com/kongwanbianjinyu/SMCEvolve.

### [65] [Context Pruning for Coding Agents via Multi-Rubric Latent Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15315v1)
*Jingjing Wang,Xiwen Chen,Wenhui Zhu,Huayu Li,Zhengxiao He,Feiyang Cai,Ana S. Carreon-Rascon,Xuanzhao Dong,Feng Luo*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 编码agent上下文剪枝，多标准隐式推理，节省token并提升agent任务性能，直接相关。

TL;DR: 提出LaMR，将代码相关性分解为语义证据和依赖支持两个维度的结构化剪枝框架，通过多标准CRF和混合专家门控实现更好的上下文压缩，在多个代码基准上提升性能并节省token。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有单目标序列标注器将所有相关性方面压缩为一个分数和一个转移矩阵，造成建模瓶颈，无法处理异质性保留模式（如连续语义跨度和稀疏结构支撑行）。

Method: 将代码相关性分解为语义证据和依赖支持两个可解释维度，每个维度用具有特定转移动态的专用CRF建模；混合专家门控网络根据查询动态加权每个维度的发射；最终CRF层融合产生保留或剪枝决策。利用AST分析从现有训练语料自动生成多标准标签并去噪。

Result: 在SWE-Bench Verified、SWE-QA、LCC、LongCodeQA四个基准上，LaMR在16个多轮比较中赢得12个，多轮任务节省token高达31%，单轮任务精确匹配提升+3.5，性能常超过全上下文基线。

Conclusion: LaMR通过去噪上下文和结构化剪枝有效提升代码智能体性能，token节省显著，性能下降微小。

中文摘要：LLM驱动的编码智能体将大部分token预算用于读取仓库文件，然而许多检索到的代码与当前任务无关。现有的学习型剪枝器使用单目标序列标注器压缩此上下文，将所有代码相关性方面压缩为一个分数和一个转移矩阵。我们表明这种公式化造成了建模瓶颈：单个CRF转移先验必须服务于异质性保留模式，包括连续语义跨度和稀疏结构支撑行。我们提出LaMR（潜在多标准），一个结构化剪枝框架，将代码相关性分解为两个可解释的质量维度，语义证据和依赖支持，每个维度由具有维度特定转移动态的专用CRF建模。混合专家门控网络根据查询动态加权每个标准的发射，而最终CRF层在融合的发射上产生聚合的保留或剪枝决策。为了在无需额外标注成本的情况下监督每个维度，我们通过基于AST的程序分析从现有训练语料中推导多标准标签，同时去噪教师的二元标签。通过有效过滤干扰噪声，LaMR经常匹配甚至超越未剪枝的全上下文基线。在四个基准测试（SWE-Bench Verified， SWE-QA， LCC， LongCodeQA）上的实验表明，LaMR在16个一对一多轮比较中赢得12个。它在多轮智能体任务上节省高达31%的更多token，在单轮任务上提高精确匹配高达+3.5，同时性能通常通过去噪上下文而增强，任何剩余的下降都是微小的。

Original abstract: LLM-powered coding agents spend the majority of their token budget reading repository files, yet much of the retrieved code is irrelevant to the task at hand. Existing learned pruners compress this context with a single-objective sequence labeler, collapsing all facets of code relevance into one score and one transition matrix. We show that this formulation creates a modeling bottleneck: a single CRF transition prior must serve heterogeneous retention patterns, including contiguous semantic spans and sparse structural support lines. We propose LaMR (Latent Multi-Rubric), a structured pruning framework that decomposes code relevance into two interpretable quality dimensions, semantic evidence and dependency support, each modeled by a dedicated CRF with dimension-specific transition dynamics. A mixture-of-experts gating network dynamically weights the per-rubric emissions conditioned on the query, and a final CRF layer on the fused emissions produces the aggregate keep-or-prune decision. To supervise each dimension without additional annotation cost, we derive multi-rubric labels from the existing training corpus via AST-based program analysis, simultaneously denoising the teacher's binary labels. By effectively filtering distracting noise, LaMR frequently matches or even outperforms unpruned full-context baselines. Experiments on four benchmarks (SWE-Bench Verified, SWE-QA, LCC, LongCodeQA) show that LaMR wins 12 of 16 head-to-head multi-turn comparisons. It saves up to 31% more tokens on multi-turn agent tasks and improves Exact Match by up to +3.5 on single-turn tasks, while performance is frequently enhanced by denoising the context, and any remaining drops are marginal.

</details>

*Kin Max Piamolini Gusmão,Nathan Gavenski,Nir Oren,Felipe Meneguzzi*

TL;DR: 本文首次系统评估了LLM在经典PDDL基准上的零样本目标识别能力，发现模型表现不均衡：部分模型能随证据提升准确性，而另一些则固守先验知识。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目标识别作为溯因任务更适合LLM利用世界知识，而现有研究缺乏对LLM在此任务上能力的系统评估。

Method: 在经典PDDL基准上对前沿LLM进行零样本目标识别评估，并通过推理轨迹的定性分析对比模型表现差异。

Result: 部分LLM随观测证据增加接近基于地标的准确率，而其他模型始终依赖世界知识先验，表明差异源于证据整合能力。

Conclusion: 目标识别可作为评估LLM基础规划知识的原则性基准，揭示其推理能力的根本差异。

中文摘要：大型语言模型最近在著名的规划领域已达到与经典规划器近乎持平的水平，然而这种能力依赖于对世界知识的利用而非真正的符号推理。目标识别是一项互补的溯因任务，在结构上更适合LLM的优势：它包括评估与世界知识的一致性，而不是生成新颖的动作序列。本文首次对前沿LLM作为目标识别器在关键经典PDDL基准上进行了系统的零样本评估。我们的结果表明，LLM在目标识别上的能力是不均衡的：一些模型随着证据积累而扩展，并在完整观测下接近基于地标的准确性，而另一些模型则无论证据积累多少，都固守于世界知识先验。对模型推理轨迹的定性分析揭示，这种差异反映了证据整合中的根本性差异，而非领域熟悉度。这些发现将目标识别定位为LLM基础规划知识的一个原则性基准。

Original abstract: Large language models have recently reached near-parity with classical planners on well-known planning domains, yet this competence relies on world-knowledge exploitation rather than genuine symbolic reasoning. Goal recognition is a complementary abductive task structurally better suited to LLM strengths: it consists of evaluating consistency with world knowledge rather than generating novel action sequences. This paper provides the first systematic zero-shot evaluation of frontier LLMs as goal recognisers on key classical PDDL benchmarks. Our results show that LLM competence on goal recognition is uneven: some models scale with evidence and approach landmark-based accuracy at full observations, while others remain anchored to world-knowledge priors regardless of how much evidence accumulates. Qualitative analysis of model reasoning traces reveals that this divergence reflects a fundamental difference in evidence integration rather than domain familiarity. These findings position goal recognition as a principled benchmark for the foundational planning knowledge of LLMs.

### [67] [Belief Engine: Configurable and Inspectable Stance Dynamics in Multi-Agent LLM Deliberation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15343v1)
*Joshua C. Yang,Maurice Flechtner,Damian Dailisan,Michiel A. Bakker*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent立场动态的可配置框架，通用多agent方法。

TL;DR: 提出信念引擎（BE），通过可审计的信念更新层和参数控制（证据采纳率u、锚定a）模拟LLM智能体在商议中的立场变化，并在DEBATE数据集上验证其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体生成的对话无法揭示立场变化的原因（如证据采纳、锚定等），缺乏可解释性和可控性。

Method: 设计信念引擎（BE），将信念表示为证据状态，通过提取论据、结构化记忆和log-odds更新规则（参数u和a控制）更新立场，支持审计轨迹。

Result: 在多个LLM上参数扫描表明u和a可靠地塑造立场动态；在DEBATE数据集中，BE能重建遵循证据的参与者立场，而稳定或对立案例指向锚定或其他因素。

Conclusion: BE为研究证据驱动的商议提供了可配置基础设施，将开放性、承诺等行为与显式更新假设关联，避免隐藏的提示效应。

中文摘要：基于LLM的智能体越来越多地被用于模拟商议性互动，如谈判、冲突解决和多轮意见交换。然而，生成的对话记录通常不揭示智能体立场变化的原因：这种变化可能反映证据采纳、锚定、角色漂移、回声效应或提示与检索上下文的变化。我们引入了信念引擎（Belief Engine, BE），这是一个可审计的信念更新层，它将“信念”视为关于某个命题的证据状态，并将其暴露为标量立场。BE将论据提取到结构化记忆中，并通过由证据采纳率u和先前锚定a控制的对数几率规则更新立场。在多个基础LLM上，参数扫描表明这些控制能够可靠地塑造立场动态，同时保留证据级别的更新轨迹。在DEBATE数据集（一个包含事前/事后意见的人类商议数据集）上，BE最佳地重建了那些最终立场遵循提取证据的参与者；而稳定和证据对立的案例则指向锚定或提取证据流之外的因素。BE为研究基于证据的商议提供了可配置的基础设施，其中开放性、承诺、趋同和分歧可以与明确的更新假设联系起来，而不是隐藏的提示效应。

Original abstract: LLM-based agents are increasingly used to simulate deliberative interactions such as negotiation, conflict resolution, and multi-turn opinion exchange. Yet generated transcripts often do not reveal why an agent's stance changes: movement may reflect evidence uptake, anchoring, role drift, echoing, or changed prompt and retrieval context. We introduce the Belief Engine (BE), an auditable belief-update layer that treats "belief" as an evidential state over a proposition and exposes it as scalar stance. BE extracts arguments into structured memory and updates stance with a log-odds rule controlled by evidence uptake u and prior anchoring a. Across multiple base LLMs, parameter sweeps show that these controls reliably shape stance dynamics while preserving an evidence-level update trail. On DEBATE, a human deliberation dataset with pre/post opinions, BE best reconstructs participants whose final stance follows extracted evidence; stable and evidence-opposed cases instead point to anchoring or factors outside the extracted evidence stream. BE provides configurable infrastructure for studying evidence-grounded deliberation, where openness, commitment, convergence, and disagreement can be tied to explicit update assumptions rather than hidden prompt effects.

### [68] [Ensemble Monitoring for AI Control: Diverse Signals Outweigh More Compute](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15377v2)
*Eugene Koran,Yejun Yun,Samantha Tetef,Benjamin Arnav,Pablo Bernabeu-Pérez*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: agent行为监控的集成方法，直接贡献于agent安全控制。

TL;DR: 通过组合多样化的监控器集成（而非单纯增加规模），可以显著提高对AI代理不安全行为的检测性能，微调监控器尤其有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI代理大规模部署需要可靠的安全监控，但构建单个强大监控器困难且人工监督不可行，迫切需要自动化且高效的检测方法。

Method: 使用12个GPT-4.1-Mini监控器（基于提示和微调策略），在编码任务（候选方案通过标准测试但对抗输入失败）上评估单个及集成性能，构建多样和同质集成进行对比。

Result: 多样集成检测性能优于单个和同质集成，最佳3监控器集成比同质集成性能提升2.4倍，并在独立数据集上表现强劲；微调监控器在所有最佳集成中出现并泛化到分布外攻击。

Conclusion: 多样性（而非规模）是性能提升的关键，集成监控是实用且经济的AI安全控制策略，微调可增强提示无法获得的检测能力。

中文摘要：随着AI系统在自主代理场景中大规模部署，确保它们采取的行动安全且符合用户意图变得重要。监控代理行为是一个关键的安全机制，然而可靠的监控器仍然难以构建，并且这些系统的规模使得人工监督不切实际。我们表明，将来自不同监控器的信号组合成集成，能够改进对错误对齐行为的检测。我们使用提示和微调策略构建了12个GPT-4.1-Mini监控器。我们在编码任务上评估它们，其中候选解决方案通过了标准测试但在对抗性输入上失败。在这种设置中，多样集成优于单个监控器和同质集成。我们最好的3监控器集成与由三个相同监控器组成的集成相比，实现了2.4倍的检测性能提升，同样的集成在独立数据集上表现强劲。我们认为这些结果表明，多样性——而非规模——驱动了增益。最佳集成结合了强大的个体性能和监控器之间的低相关性。此外，微调后的监控器出现在每个表现最佳的集成中，并在分布外攻击类型上保持这一优势，这表明微调能够实现仅靠提示无法引发的检测能力。这些结果支持集成监控作为一种实用的AI控制策略，以合理的推理成本获得安全增益。

Original abstract: As AI systems are increasingly deployed in autonomous agentic settings at scale, it is important to ensure the actions they take are safe and aligned with user intent. Monitoring agent actions is a key safety mechanism, yet reliable monitors remain difficult to build and the scale of these systems makes human oversight impractical. We show that combining signals from diverse monitors into an ensemble improves detection of misaligned actions. We build 12 GPT-4.1-Mini monitors using both prompting and fine-tuning strategies. We evaluate them on coding tasks where candidate solutions pass standard tests but fail on adversarial inputs. In this setting, diverse ensembles outperform both individual monitors and homogeneous ensembles. Our best 3-monitor ensemble achieves 2.4x greater detection performance gain compared to an ensemble composed of three identical monitors, with the same ensemble performing strongly on an independent dataset. We contend that these results show that diversity - not scale - drives gains. The best ensembles combine strong individual performance with low correlation between monitors. Furthermore, fine-tuned monitors appear in every top-performing ensemble and maintain this advantage on out-of-distribution attack types, suggesting that fine-tuning enables detection capabilities that prompting alone does not elicit. These results support ensemble monitoring as a practical AI control strategy for safety gains at reasonable inference costs.

### [69] [Beyond Partner Diversity: An Influence-Based Team Steering Framework for Zero-Shot Human-Machine Teaming](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15400v1)
*Wei Sheng,Rohan Paleja*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 人机团队零样本协调框架，通用多agent协作方法。

TL;DR: 提出基于影响的团队引导（IBTS）框架，通过影响塑造激励代理发现多样化的协调模式并引导轨迹，在Overcooked-AI的两代理、三代理及首次人类实验中提升团队性能，表明扩展零样本协调需结合协调机制和伙伴覆盖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 零样本协调在团队规模扩大和通信退化时仅靠伙伴覆盖不足，需要引入影响塑造以引导代理发现并转向更强的协调模式。

Method: 提出IBTS框架，使用影响塑造（influence shaping）来激励代理探索多样化的团队交互模式，并对正在进行的轨迹进行引导，使其收敛到高性能的协调模式。

Result: 在Overcooked-AI上，包括双代理、三代理模拟以及30名受试者的人机团队实验，IBTS均提升了团队性能，优于多种基线方法。

Conclusion: 扩展零样本协调需要将稀疏奖励协调机制与伙伴变化覆盖相结合，而非仅依赖伙伴多样性。

中文摘要：虽然AI代理正在从孤立工具迅速演进为交互式协作者，但数据驱动的人机团队协作（HMT）方法仍然成本高昂，因为它们依赖于跨领域、队友和团队规模的人类交互数据。零样本协调（ZSC）通过模拟多样化的伙伴群体来近似未见过伙伴的行为，从而解决了这一瓶颈。然而，随着团队规模扩大和通信退化，仅靠伙伴覆盖是不够的。为了解决这一不足，我们提出了基于影响的团队引导（IBTS），该框架利用影响塑造来激励代理发现多样化、高性能的团队交互模式，并进一步引导正在进行的轨迹朝着更强的学习协调模式发展。我们在Overcooked-AI上评估了IBTS，包括双代理和三代理设置，从而测试学习到的协调结构是否超越了二元交互。我们的评估包括模拟伙伴、合成伙伴风格变化，以及据我们所知的首次30名受试者的Overcooked-AI HMT研究，其中涉及两个真实人类队友和一个机器队友。在这些评估中，IBTS提升了团队性能，优于竞争基线，突显了扩展ZSC需要将稀疏奖励协调机制与伙伴变化覆盖相结合，而不是仅仅依赖多样性。

Original abstract: While AI agents are rapidly advancing from isolated tools to interactive collaborators, data-driven human-machine teaming (HMT) methods remain costly in their reliance on human interaction data across domains, teammates, and team sizes. Zero-shot coordination (ZSC) addresses this bottleneck by simulating diverse partner populations to approximate how unseen partners might behave. However, partner coverage alone is insufficient as team settings scale and communication becomes degraded. To remedy this deficiency, we propose Influence-Based Team Steering (IBTS), a framework that uses influence shaping to incentivize agents to discover diverse, high-performing team interaction patterns and further steers ongoing trajectories toward stronger learned coordination modes. We assess IBTS on Overcooked-AI in both two-agent and three-agent settings, allowing us to test whether learned coordination structure transfers beyond dyadic interaction. Our evaluation includes simulated partners, synthetic partner-style variation, and, to our knowledge, the first 30-subject Overcooked-AI HMT study involving two real human teammates and one machine teammate. Across these evaluations, IBTS improves team performance against competing baselines, highlighting the need for scaled ZSC to combine sparse-reward coordination mechanisms with partner-variation coverage rather than relying on diversity alone.

</details>

### [70] [Contestable Multi-Agent Debate with Arena-based Argumentative Computation for Multimedia Verification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14495v1)
*Truong Thanh Hung Nguyen,Vo Thanh Khang Nguyen,Hoang-Loc Cao,Phuc Ho,Van Pham,Hung Cao*

Main category: cs.MM

Selection reason: 多智能体辩论框架，涉及论证计算与争议解决，通用多Agent协作方法可迁移

TL;DR: 提出了一个结合多模态大模型、外部工具和A-QBAF的可争辩多智能体框架，用于多媒体验证，生成透明、可编辑的章节验证报告。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多媒体验证需要透明和可争辩的推理，而不仅仅是准确的结论。

Method: 将案例分解为声明为中心的章节，检索证据，转化为具有出处和强度分数的支持/攻击论点，通过小型局部论证图、选择性冲突解决和不确定性感知升级进行推理。

Result: 生成了透明、可编辑且计算实用的逐章节验证报告。

Conclusion: 该框架适用于实际多媒体验证，代码已公开。

中文摘要：多媒体验证不仅需要准确的结论，还需要透明和可争辩的推理。我们提出了一个可争辩的多智能体框架，集成了多模态大语言模型、外部验证工具和基于竞技场的定量双极论证（A-QBAF），作为对ICMR 2026多媒体验证大挑战的提交。我们的方法将每个案例分解为以声明为中心的章节，检索有针对性的证据，并将证据转化为具有出处和强度分数的结构化支持和攻击论点。这些论点通过小型局部论证图、选择性冲突解决和不确定性感知升级来解决。生成的系统生成逐章节的验证报告，这些报告是透明的、可编辑的，并且对于实际多媒体验证在计算上是实用的。我们的实现公开在：https://github.com/Analytics-Everywhere-Lab/MV2026_the_liems。

Original abstract: Multimedia verification requires not only accurate conclusions but also transparent and contestable reasoning. We propose a contestable multi-agent framework that integrates multimodal large language models, external verification tools, and arena-based quantitative bipolar argumentation (A-QBAF) as a submission to the ICMR 2026 Grand Challenge on Multimedia Verification. Our method decomposes each case into claim-centered sections, retrieves targeted evidence, and converts evidence into structured support and attack arguments with provenance and strength scores. These arguments are resolved through small local argument graphs with selective clash resolution and uncertainty-aware escalation. The resulting system generates section-wise verification reports that are transparent, editable, and computationally practical for real-world multimedia verification. Our implementation is public at: https://github.com/Analytics-Everywhere-Lab/MV2026_the_liems.

### [71] [IntentVLA: Short-Horizon Intent Modeling for Aliased Robot Manipulation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14712v2)
*Shijie Lian,Bin Yu,Xiaopeng Lin,Zhaolong Shen,Laurence Tianruo Yang,Yurun Jin,Haishan Liu,Changti Wu,Hang Yuan,Cong Huang,Kai Chen*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 提出历史条件VLA框架处理观察混叠，对agent短期意图建模有启发。

TL;DR: 提出IntentVLA框架，通过历史条件解决机器人模仿学习中的观测歧义问题，提升执行稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA策略因仅依赖当前观测，在部分可观测下产生片段间冲突，导致不稳定执行。

Method: 提出IntentVLA，编码历史视觉信息为短期意图表示来条件化片段生成；并构建AliasBench基准以隔离观测歧义。

Result: 在AliasBench、SimplerEnv、LIBERO和RoboCasa上，IntentVLA提升了卷展稳定性并超越强VLA基线。

Conclusion: IntentVLA有效缓解观测歧义问题，提升机器人模仿学习的稳定性。

中文摘要：机器人模仿数据通常是多模态的：相似的视觉-语言观测可能跟随不同的动作片段，因为人类演示者以不同的短期意图、任务阶段或近期背景行动。现有的基于帧条件的VLA策略仅从当前观测和指令推断每个片段，因此在部分可观测性下，它们可能在相邻的重新规划步骤中重新采样不同的意图，导致片段间冲突和不稳定的执行。我们引入了IntentVLA，一种历史条件VLA框架，它将最近的视觉观测编码为紧凑的短期意图表示，并用于条件化片段生成。我们还引入了AliasBench，一个在RoboTwin2上的12任务歧义感知基准，具有匹配的训练数据和评估环境，以隔离短期观测歧义。在AliasBench、SimplerEnv、LIBERO和RoboCasa上，IntentVLA提高了卷展稳定性，并超越了强VLA基线。

Original abstract: Robot imitation data are often multimodal: similar visual-language observations may be followed by different action chunks because human demonstrators act with different short-horizon intents, task phases, or recent context. Existing frame-conditioned VLA policies infer each chunk from the current observation and instruction alone, so under partial observability they may resample different intents across adjacent replanning steps, leading to inter-chunk conflict and unstable execution. We introduce IntentVLA, a history-conditioned VLA framework that encodes recent visual observations into a compact short-horizon intent representation and uses it to condition chunk generation. We further introduce AliasBench, a 12-task ambiguity-aware benchmark on RoboTwin2 with matched training data and evaluation environments that isolate short-horizon observation aliasing. Across AliasBench, SimplerEnv, LIBERO, and RoboCasa, IntentVLA improves rollout stability and outperforms strong VLA baselines

</details>


### [72] [CLOVER: Closed-Loop Value Estimation and Ranking for End-to-End Autonomous Driving Planning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15120v2)
*Sining Ang,Yuguang Yang,Canyu Chen,Yan Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 自动驾驶规划框架，但生成-评分与闭环自蒸馏可迁移至agent设计

TL;DR: CLOVER通过构建伪专家轨迹、集合级覆盖训练和闭环蒸馏，解决了端到端自动驾驶规划中模仿学习与规则评估不匹配的问题，在多个基准上达到最优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有端到端规划器因训练（单轨迹模仿）与评估（规则指标）不匹配，导致靠近记录的轨迹可能违反规则，而远离的轨迹可能更好，特别是在提议选择型规划器中问题更突出。

Method: CLOVER框架包含生成器（生成多样化候选轨迹）和评分器（预测规划子分数）。通过评估器过滤构造伪专家轨迹进行集合级覆盖训练，再进行保守闭环自蒸馏：评分器拟合真实评估器分数，生成器以教师选择top-k和向量帕累托目标优化并加稳定性正则化。

Result: 在NAVSIM上PDMS 94.5/EPDMS 90.4；NavHard上EPDMS 48.3持平最强；nuScenes开环评估L2误差和碰撞率最低。

Conclusion: CLOVER通过闭环蒸馏和集合级训练有效缓解了训练-评估不匹配，提升了规划性能，且不完美评分器也能可靠改进生成器。

中文摘要：端到端自动驾驶规划器通常通过模仿单个记录轨迹进行训练，但通过基于规则的规划指标进行评估，这些指标衡量安全性、可行性、进展和舒适性。这造成了训练与评估的不匹配：靠近记录路径的轨迹可能违反规划规则，而距离演示较远的替代轨迹可能仍然有效且得分较高。这种不匹配对于提议选择型规划器尤其有限，因为其性能取决于候选集覆盖率和评分器排名质量。我们提出CLOVER，一种用于端到端自动驾驶规划的闭环价值估计与排名框架。CLOVER遵循轻量级生成器-评分器公式：生成器生成多样化的候选轨迹，评分器预测规划指标子分数以在推理时对其进行排名。为了将提议支持扩展到单个轨迹模仿之外，CLOVER构建了评估器过滤的伪专家轨迹，并以集合级覆盖监督训练生成器。然后它执行保守的闭环自蒸馏：评分器拟合生成提议上真实评估器子分数，而生成器通过教师选择的top-k和向量帕累托目标与稳定性正则化进行优化。我们分析了不完美的评分器何时可以改进生成器，表明当评分器选择的目标在真实评估器下丰富且更新保持保守时，评分器介导的优化是可靠的。在NAVSIM上，CLOVER实现了94.5 PDMS和90.4 EPDMS，建立了新的最佳性能。在更具挑战性的NavHard分割上，它获得了48.3 EPDMS，与最强报告结果相匹配。在补充的nuScenes开环评估中，CLOVER在比较方法中实现了最低的L2误差和碰撞率。代码和数据将在https://github.com/WilliamXuanYu/CLOVER发布。

Original abstract: End-to-end autonomous driving planners are commonly trained by imitating a single logged trajectory, yet evaluated by rule-based planning metrics that measure safety, feasibility, progress, and comfort. This creates a training--evaluation mismatch: trajectories close to the logged path may violate planning rules, while alternatives farther from the demonstration can remain valid and high-scoring. The mismatch is especially limiting for proposal-selection planners, whose performance depends on candidate-set coverage and scorer ranking quality. We propose CLOVER, a Closed-LOop Value Estimation and Ranking framework for end-to-end autonomous driving planning. CLOVER follows a lightweight generator--scorer formulation: a generator produces diverse candidate trajectories, and a scorer predicts planning-metric sub-scores to rank them at inference time. To expand proposal support beyond single-trajectory imitation, CLOVER constructs evaluator-filtered pseudo-expert trajectories and trains the generator with set-level coverage supervision. It then performs conservative closed-loop self-distillation: the scorer is fitted to true evaluator sub-scores on generated proposals, while the generator is refined toward teacher-selected top-$k$ and vector-Pareto targets with stability regularization. We analyze when an imperfect scorer can improve the generator, showing that scorer-mediated refinement is reliable when scorer-selected targets are enriched under the true evaluator and updates remain conservative. On NAVSIM, CLOVER achieves 94.5 PDMS and 90.4 EPDMS, establishing a new state of the art. On the more challenging NavHard split, it obtains 48.3 EPDMS, matching the strongest reported result. On supplementary nuScenes open-loop evaluation, CLOVER achieves the lowest L2 error and collision rate among compared methods. Code data will be released at https://github.com/WilliamXuanYu/CLOVER.

</details>


### [73] [Pelican-Unify 1.0: A Unified Embodied Intelligence Model for Understanding, Reasoning, Imagination and Action](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15153v2)
*Yi Zhang,Yinda Chen,Che Liu,Zeyuan Ding,Jin Xu,Shilong Zou,Junwei Liao,Jiayu Hu,Xiancong Ren,Xiaopeng Zhang,Yechi Liu,Haoyuan Shi,Zecong Tang,Haosong Sun,Renwen Cui,Kuishu Wu,Wenhai Liu,Yang Xu,Yingji Zhang,Yidong Wang,Senkang Hu,Jinpeng Lu,Nga Teng Chan,Yechen Wu,Zeting Liu,Xianzhou Hou,Yong Dai,Jian Tang,Xiaozhu Ju*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 具身智能统一模型，但统一架构思想可启发通用agent设计

TL;DR: 提出统一化具身基础模型Pelican-Unify 1.0，使用单个VLM联合优化理解、推理、未来生成和动作，在多个基准上取得领先性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前具身智能模型通常将理解、推理、想象和动作分离为独立模块，缺乏联合优化，希望通过统一化证明可以同时提升所有能力而不妥协。

Method: 使用单个VLM作为统一的理解和推理模块，生成共享潜变量，再由统一未来生成器（UFG）联合生成未来视频和未来动作，所有损失反向传播到共享表示。

Result: 在八个VLM基准上达到64.7（同类最佳），WorldArena 66.03（第一），RoboTwin 93.5（第二好），证明统一模型保持专家强度。

Conclusion: 统一化范式成功将理解、推理、想象和动作整合到一个模型中，且性能不降低，为具身智能模型设计提供了新方向。

中文摘要：我们提出Pelican-Unify 1.0，这是第一个根据统一化原则训练的具身基础模型。Pelican-Unify 1.0使用单个VLM作为统一的理解模块，将场景、指令、视觉上下文和动作历史映射到共享语义空间。同一个VLM还作为统一的推理模块，在单次前向传播中自回归地产生任务、动作和面向未来的思维链，并将最终隐藏状态投影为密集潜变量。然后，一个统一未来生成器(UFG)以该潜变量为条件，在同一去噪过程中通过两个模态特定的输出头联合生成未来视频和未来动作。语言、视频和动作损失都反向传播到共享表示中，使模型能够在训练期间联合优化理解、推理、想象和动作，而不是训练三个孤立的专家系统。实验表明，统一并不意味着妥协。使用单个检查点，Pelican-Unify 1.0在所有三个能力上均表现强劲：在八个VLM基准测试中达到64.7，在可比规模的模型中最佳；在WorldArena上达到66.03，排名第一；在RoboTwin上达到93.5，在比较的动作方法中平均排名第二。这些结果表明，统一范式在保持专家强度的同时，将理解、推理、想象和动作整合到一个模型中。

Original abstract: We present Pelican-Unify 1.0, the first embodied foundation model trained according to the principle of unification. Pelican-Unify 1.0 uses a single VLM as a unified understanding module, mapping scenes, instructions, visual contexts, and action histories into a shared semantic space. The same VLM also serves as a unified reasoning module, autoregressively producing task-, action-, and future-oriented chains of thought in a single forward pass and projecting the final hidden state into a dense latent variable. A Unified Future Generator (UFG) then conditions on this latent variable and jointly generates future videos and future actions through two modality-specific output heads within the same denoising process. The language, video, and action losses are all backpropagated into the shared representation, enabling the model to jointly optimize understanding, reasoning, imagination, and action during training, rather than training three isolated expert systems.
  Experiments demonstrate that unification does not imply compromise. With a single checkpoint, Pelican-Unify 1.0 achieves strong performance across all three capabilities: 64.7 on eight VLM benchmarks, the best among comparable-scale models; 66.03 on WorldArena, ranking first; and 93.5 on RoboTwin, the second-best average among compared action methods. These results show that the unified paradigm succeeds in preserving specialist strength while bringing understanding, reasoning, imagination, and action into one model.

</details>

# cs.CR [[Back]](#toc)

### [74] [Web Agents Should Adopt the Plan-Then-Execute Paradigm](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14290v1)
*Julien Piet,Annabella Chow,Yiwei Hou,Muxi Lyu,Sylvie Venuto,Jinhao Zhu,Raluca Ada Popa,David Wagner*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 网络代理应默认采用计划-然后-执行架构而非ReAct，因为ReAct易受提示注入攻击，而计划-然后-执行可防止不可信数据改变控制流，且WebArena所有任务兼容该架构，但需要类型化接口来支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ReAct架构中，网络内容直接流入模型决定动作，容易导致提示注入攻击，因此需要更安全的架构。

Method: 提出计划-然后-执行架构，在观察运行时内容前预定义任务程序；分析WebArena基准测试验证兼容性；识别采用该架构的障碍。

Result: WebArena所有任务与计划-然后-执行兼容，80%可纯程序化完成；主要障碍是浏览器工具缺乏语义映射和预知效果。

Conclusion: 网络代理需要类型化、完整、可审计的网站API来实现计划-然后-执行，这是基础设施问题而非建模问题。

中文摘要：ReAct已成为跨LLM代理的默认架构，许多现有的网络代理都遵循这一范式。我们认为这对于网络代理来说是错误的默认选择。相反，网络代理应默认采用计划-然后-执行的模式：在观察运行时网络内容之前，承诺一个特定于任务的程序，然后执行它。原因是网络内容混合了来自多方的输入。一个电商产品页面可能结合了卖家的列表、客户评论和赞助广告。在ReAct下，所有这些内容在决定下一步动作时都会流入模型，为提示注入提供了直接路径，从而控制代理的控制流。计划-然后-执行改变了这一边界：不可信数据可能影响预定义执行图内的值或分支，但它不能重新定义用户任务或导致模型在运行时合成新动作。我们分析了WebArena（一个流行的网络代理基准测试），发现所有任务都与计划-然后-执行兼容，而80%的任务可以通过纯程序化计划完成，无需任何运行时LLM子程序。我们确定了在网络中采用计划-然后-执行的主要障碍：要使其良好运行，工具必须清晰地映射到语义动作，且效果在执行前已知，这样代理才有足够的信息进行规划。网络并未自然暴露这一接口。浏览器工具如点击、打字和滚动具有依赖于页面的含义。在此层面进行规划是短视的：代理只能看到当前页面上的动作，后续动作只有在执行后才出现。缩小这一差距需要类型化接口，将网站交互从点击和按键转变为任务级操作。这是一个基础设施问题，而非建模问题。网络任务默认不需要反应性；它们需要类型化、完整、可审计的网站API。

Original abstract: ReAct has become the default architecture across LLM agents, and many existing web agents follow this paradigm. We argue that it is the wrong default for web agents. Instead, web agents should default to plan-then-execute: commit to a task-specific program before observing runtime web content, then execute it. The reason is that web content mixes inputs from many parties. An e-commerce product page may combine a seller's listing, customer reviews and sponsored advertisements. Under ReAct, all of this content flows into the model when deciding on the next action, creating a direct path for prompt injections to steer the agent's control flow. Plan-then-execute changes this boundary: untrusted data may influence values or branches inside a predefined execution graph, but it cannot redefine the user task or cause the model to synthesize new actions at runtime. We analyze WebArena, a popular web agent benchmark, and find that all tasks are compatible with plan-then-execute, while 80% can be completed with a purely programmatic plan, without any runtime LLM subroutine. We identify the main barrier to adopting plan-then-execute on the web: For it to work well, tools must map cleanly to semantic actions, with effects known before execution, so agents have enough information to plan. The web does not naturally expose that interface. Browser tools such as click, type, and scroll have page-dependent meanings. Planning at this layer is near-sighted: the agent can only see actions on the current page, and later actions appear only after it acts. Closing this gap requires typed interfaces that turn website interactions from clicks and keystrokes to task-level operations. This is an infrastructure problem, not a modeling problem. Web tasks do not need reactivity by default; they need typed, complete, auditable website APIs.

</details>


### [75] [MemLineage: Lineage-Guided Enforcement for LLM Agent Memory](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14421v1)
*Ciyan Ouyang,Rui Hou*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 提出LLM agent记忆的防御框架，涉及记忆安全与追溯，对agent设计有直接启发。

TL;DR: MemLineage是一种为LLM智能体记忆提供加密来源和推导谱系的防御机制，通过链式追溯防止记忆中毒攻击，在测试中实现零攻击成功率，且开销极低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 防止不可信内容通过持久化智能体状态注入后续会话，用于敏感操作，同时保留有用记忆。

Method: 基于RFC-6962 Merkle日志和Ed25519签名，使用加权推导DAG记录记忆来源，通过最大强边传播规则实现不可信路径持久性，并由敏感动作门拒绝来自外部祖先的调度。

Result: 在三种记忆中毒工作负载下，MemLineage在确定性测试台上实现零ASR，亚毫秒级开销；在AgentDojo基准测试中，所有配置下严格ASR降至零。

Conclusion: MemLineage有效防御LLM智能体记忆中毒攻击，且性能开销低，具有可审计性。

中文摘要：我们提出MemLineage，一种针对LLM智能体记忆的防御机制，它为每条记忆附加了加密来源和LLM介导的推导谱系。近期和同期的工作表明，不可信内容可能被写入持久化智能体状态，并在后续会话中作为指令重新进入；剩下的系统问题是如何在保留有用记忆回忆的同时，防止此类状态为敏感操作提供理由。MemLineage将此视为链式保管问题而非过滤问题。它基于RFC-6962 Merkle日志和每主体Ed25519签名条目设计了六个模块：一个加权推导有向无环图（DAG）记录哪些检索到的条目影响了每条新记忆，而最大强边传播规则使得任何其归属边保持在阈值以上的链都满足“不可信路径持久性”。敏感动作门随后拒绝其活动理由来源于外部祖先的调度，同时允许良性回忆。我们在确定性机制隔离测试台上评估了三种防御单元对抗三种记忆中毒工作负载；在该测试台中，MemLineage是唯一将所有三列的ASR（攻击成功率）降至零的配置，而亚毫秒级每操作开销使其远低于任何LLM调用的噪声基底。一个基于Codex的AgentDojo桥进一步将强模型行为与防御层行为分离：在故意设置漏洞的工具输出配置下，无防御和仅签名基线在所有六个银行配对任务上均失败，而所有MemLineage行将严格的AgentDojo ASR降至零。核心确定性工件经过字节等价CI验证；托管模型的AgentDojo和实时模型扫描记录为可审计日志而非字节固定工件。

Original abstract: We introduce MemLineage, a defense for LLM agent memory that attaches both cryptographic provenance and LLM-mediated derivation lineage to every entry. Recent and concurrent work shows that untrusted content can be written into persistent agent state and re-enter later sessions as an instruction; the remaining systems question is how to preserve useful memory recall while preventing such state from justifying sensitive actions. MemLineage treats this as a chain-of-custody problem rather than a filtering problem. It is a six-module design around an RFC-6962 Merkle log over per-principal Ed25519-signed entries: a weighted derivation DAG records which retrieved entries influenced each new memory, and a max-of-strong-edges propagation rule makes Untrusted-Path Persistence hold for any chain whose attribution edges remain above threshold. The sensitive-action gate then refuses dispatches whose active justification descends from an external ancestor, while still allowing benign recall. We evaluate three defense cells against three memory-poisoning workloads on a deterministic mechanism-isolation harness; MemLineage is the only configuration in that harness that drives all three columns to zero ASR, while sub-millisecond per-operation overhead keeps it well below the noise floor of any LLM call. A Codex-backed AgentDojo bridge further separates strong-model behavior from defense-layer behavior: under an intentionally vulnerable tool-output profile, no-defense and signature-only baselines fail on all six banking pairs, while all MemLineage rows reduce strict AgentDojo ASR to zero. The core deterministic artifacts are byte-equal CI-verified; hosted-model AgentDojo and live-model sweeps are recorded as auditable logs rather than byte-pinned artifacts.

</details>


### [76] [Exploiting LLM Agent Supply Chains via Payload-less Skills](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14460v1)
*Xinyu Liu,Yukai Zhao,Xing Hu,Xin Xia*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出语义合规劫持（SCH）攻击，通过将恶意目标转化为自然语言合规规则，使LLM自主代理生成并执行未授权代码，成功逃避现有检测，最高攻击成功率达77.67%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全审计机制只能检测显式代码注入和预定义威胁，无法识别通过代理动态合成的恶意行为，存在安全盲点。

Method: 开发SCH方法，将恶意目标转化为非结构化自然语言指令作为合规规则，利用代理的生成能力执行未授权代码；并引入MS-AO优化攻击效果。

Result: 在多种配置下，SCH对机密性破坏和RCE的成功率分别达77.67%和67.33%，且被操纵的技能文件检测率为0.00%。

Conclusion: 揭示代理供应链中未探索的攻击面，需从签名检测转向语义意图验证。

中文摘要：由大型语言模型（LLM）驱动的自主代理通过开放市场中的第三方技能获取外部功能。采用这些集成扩大了潜在的攻击面，促使需要进行系统的安全评估。当前的审计机制能够通过安全扫描有效识别显式的代码负载和预定义的威胁内容。如果恶意行为缺乏直接注入，而是通过代理固有的生成能力在运行时动态合成，这些检测机制就会被绕过。为探索这一盲点，我们引入了语义合规劫持（SCH），这是一种针对自主编码环境的无负载供应链攻击。SCH方法将恶意目标转化为非结构化的自然语言指令，格式化为必要的合规规则，导致代理生成并执行未经授权的代码。为评估此攻击的现实可行性，我们开发了一个自动化流水线，在由三种主流代理框架和三种不同基础模型组成的测试矩阵上，使用情境化场景评估其有效性。研究结果表明了这种威胁的普遍性，在最易受攻击的配置下，SCH在机密性破坏方面达到了高达77.67%的成功率，远程代码执行（RCE）方面达到了67.33%的成功率。此外，多技能自动优化（MS-AO）的引入进一步提升了攻击效能。通过省略可识别的抽象语法树（AST）签名和显式的恶意意图，被操纵的技能文件保持了0.00%的检测率，避开了当前的扫描工具。这项研究突显了代理供应链中一个未被充分探索的攻击面，指出了从基于签名的检测模型向语义意图验证的必要转变。

Original abstract: Autonomous agents powered by Large Language Models (LLMs) acquire external functionalities through third-party skills available in open marketplaces. Adopting these integrations broadens the potential attack surface, prompting a need for systematic security evaluation. Current auditing mechanisms are effective at identifying explicit code payloads and predefined threat contents through security scanning. These detection mechanisms are bypassed if malicious behaviors lack direct injection and are instead synthesized dynamically at runtime through the agent's inherent generative capabilities. Exploring this blind spot, we introduce Semantic Compliance Hijacking (SCH), a payload-less supply chain attack targeting autonomous coding environments. The SCH approach translates malicious goals into unstructured natural language instructions formatted as necessary compliance rules, leading the agent to generate and execute unauthorized code. To assess the real-world viability of this attack, we developed an automated pipeline to evaluate its effectiveness across a test matrix comprising three mainstream agent frameworks and three distinct foundation models using contextualized scenarios. The findings demonstrate the pervasive nature of this threat, with SCH achieving peak success rates of up to 77.67% for confidentiality breaches and 67.33% for Remote Code Execution (RCE) under the most vulnerable configurations. Furthermore, the introduction of Multi-Skill Automated Optimization (MS-AO) further boosted attack efficacy. By omitting recognizable Abstract Syntax Tree (AST) signatures and explicit harmful intents, the manipulated skill files maintained a 0.00% detection rate, evading current scanning tools. This research highlights an underexplored attack surface within agent supply chains, pointing to a necessary transition from signature-based detection models toward semantic intent validation.

### [77] [Known By Their Actions: Fingerprinting LLM Browser Agents via UI Traces](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14786v1)
*William Lugoloobi,Samuelle Marro,Jabez Magomere,Joss Wright,Chris Russell*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: LLM浏览器agent指纹识别，涉及agent安全与行为分析，可迁移

TL;DR: 通过被动追踪智能体的动作和交互时间，可以高精度识别其背后的LLM模型，构成安全风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究网站能否被动识别驱动智能体的LLM模型，以揭示潜在的安全风险——针对模型已知漏洞的定向攻击。

Method: 在14个前沿LLM和4个网络环境（信息检索和购物任务）中，使用被动JavaScript跟踪器捕获智能体的动作和交互时间，训练分类器识别底层模型；并测试分类器的泛化能力、所需轨迹数量、早期识别能力以及对随机时间延迟的鲁棒性。

Result: 分类器能以高达96%的F1分数识别模型；能跨模型大小和系列泛化；少量轨迹即可训练；能在episode早期推断身份；随机时间延迟降低性能但重新训练后恢复。

Conclusion: 基于LLM的智能体在网页交互中容易被被动追踪识别模型，当前缺乏有效的防御手段，需警惕由此带来的安全威胁。

中文摘要：随着基于LLM的智能体越来越多地代表用户浏览网页，一个自然的问题出现了：网站能否被动地识别出驱动智能体的底层模型？这样做将构成重大的安全风险，使得针对已知模型漏洞进行定向攻击成为可能。在涵盖信息检索和购物任务的14个前沿LLM和四个网络环境中，我们证明，智能体的动作和交互时间（通过被动JavaScript跟踪器捕获）足以识别底层模型，F1分数高达96%。我们通过展示基于智能体动作训练的分类器能够跨模型大小和系列泛化，正式界定了这一攻击面。我们进一步表明，仅需少量交互轨迹即可训练出强大的分类器，并且可以在一个episode早期推断出智能体身份。在动作之间注入随机时间延迟会显著降低分类器性能，但不能提供稳健的保护：在延迟轨迹上重新训练的分类器在很大程度上恢复了性能。我们在此发布我们的工具包和标记的智能体轨迹语料库。

Original abstract: As LLM-based agents increasingly browse the web on users' behalf, a natural question arises: can websites passively identify which underlying model powers an agent? Doing so would represent a significant security risk, enabling targeted attacks tailored to known model vulnerabilities. Across 14 frontier LLMs and four web environments spanning information retrieval and shopping tasks, we show that an agent's actions and interaction timings, captured via a passive JavaScript tracker, are sufficient to identify the underlying model with up to 96\% F1. We formalise this attack surface by demonstrating that classifiers trained on agent actions generalise across model sizes and families. We further show that strong classifiers can be trained from few interaction traces and that agent identity can be inferred early within an episode. Injecting randomised timing delays between actions substantially degrades classifier performance, but does not provide robust protection: a classifier retrained on delayed traces largely recovers performance. We release our harness and a labelled corpus of agent traces \href{https://github.com/KabakaWilliam/known_actions}{here}.

### [78] [Do Coding Agents Understand Least-Privilege Authorization?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14859v2)
*Zheng Yan,Jingxiang Weng,Charles Chen,Dengyun Peng,Ethan Qin,Jiannan Guan,Jinhao Liu,Qiming Yu,Yixin Yuan,Fanqing Meng,Carl Che,Mengkang Hu*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 研究coding agent的权限边界推断，对安全部署有启发，间接相关代码优化agent。

TL;DR: 本文提出权限边界推断任务和AuthBench基准，发现直接策略生成是授权瓶颈，并提出充分性-紧致性分解方法，通过前向模拟和审计提升安全性和效用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 编码代理需最小权限授权以确保安全部署，但当前模型能否自行推断权限边界尚不清楚，需系统研究。

Method: 定义权限边界推断任务，构建AuthBench基准（120个任务），并提出充分性-紧致性分解：先前向模拟生成覆盖策略，再审计每个权限的依据和敏感性。

Result: AuthBench显示模型存在授权误差且推理增加不解决；分解方法在紧致性偏好模型上敏感任务成功率提升15.8%，并降低所有模型攻击成功率。

Conclusion: 直接策略生成是瓶颈，充分性-紧致性分解能有效改善授权质量，提升安全部署可行性。

中文摘要：随着编码代理获得对shell、仓库和用户文件的访问权限，最小权限授权成为安全部署的先决条件：代理应获得完成任务所需的足够权限，而不应拥有暴露敏感面的不必要权限。为了研究当前模型是否能自行推断这一边界，我们首先引入了权限边界推断，其中模型将任务指令和终端环境映射到文件级的读/写/执行策略，以及AuthBench，一个包含120个真实终端任务的基准测试，具有人工审核的权限标签和用于效用和攻击结果的可执行验证器。AuthBench显示，授权不是一个简单的保守与许可的校准问题：前沿模型常常遗漏执行链所需的权限，同时授予未使用或敏感的访问权限。增加推理时间推理并不能解决这种不匹配。相反，每个模型都趋向于一个特定于模型的授权吸引子：更多的推理使其自身的失败模式更加一致，无论是宽泛但暴露的，还是严格但脆弱的。这表明直接策略生成是瓶颈，因为单次生成必须同时发现所有必要的访问并拒绝所有不必要的访问。因此，我们提出了充分性-紧致性分解，它首先通过前向模拟任务生成覆盖导向的策略，然后审计每个授予条目的依据和敏感性。在测试的模型中，这种分解在紧致性偏好的模型上使敏感任务成功率提高了高达15.8%，同时降低了所有评估模型中的攻击成功率。

Original abstract: As coding agents gain access to shells, repositories, and user files, least-privilege authorization becomes a prerequisite for safe deployment: an agent should receive enough authority to complete the task, without unnecessary authority that exposes sensitive surfaces. To study whether current models can infer this boundary themselves, we first introduce permission-boundary inference, where a model maps a task instruction and terminal environment to a file-level read/write/execute policy, and AuthBench, a benchmark of 120 realistic terminal tasks with human-reviewed permission labels and executable validators for utility and attack outcomes. AuthBench shows that authorization is not a simple conservative-versus-permissive calibration problem: frontier models often omit permissions required by the execution chain while also granting unused or sensitive accesses. Increasing inference-time reasoning does not resolve this mismatch. Instead, each model moves toward a model-specific authorization attractor: more reasoning makes it more consistent in its own failure mode, whether broad-but-exposed or tight-but-brittle. This suggests that direct policy generation is the bottleneck, because a single generation must both discover all necessary accesses and reject all unnecessary ones. We therefore propose Sufficiency-Tightness Decomposition, which first generates a coverage-oriented policy by forward-simulating the task and then audits each granted entry for grounding and sensitivity. Across tested models, this decomposition improves sensitive-task success by up to 15.8% on tightness-biased models while reducing attack success across all evaluated models.

### [79] [WARD: Adversarially Robust Defense of Web Agents Against Prompt Injections](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15030v1)
*Tri Cao,Yulin Chen,Hieu Cao,Yibo Li,Khoi Le,Thong Nguyen,Yuexin Li,Yufei He,Yue Liu,Shuicheng Yan,Bryan Hooi*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: Web agent对抗防御，通用agent安全方法

TL;DR: 提出WARD防护模型和A3T自适应对抗训练框架，通过大规模数据集和协同进化机制，有效防御Web代理的提示注入攻击，实现高召回率、低误报率和零延迟并行部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有防护模型泛化能力差、误报率高、延迟大且易受对抗攻击，无法满足Web代理在开放环境中的安全需求。

Method: 构建大规模数据集WARD-Base（约17.7万样本）和针对防护模型的提示注入数据集WARD-PIG，提出A3T自适应对抗训练框架，通过基于记忆的攻击者与防护模型共同进化迭代增强鲁棒性。

Result: 在分布外基准上达到近乎完美召回率，保持低误报率，对针对防护模型和自适应攻击具有鲁棒性，且与代理并行运行不增加延迟。

Conclusion: WARD是一种实用、高效且鲁棒的Web代理防护模型，能够有效应对提示注入攻击，适用于安全关键的自动化任务。

中文摘要：Web代理可以通过与网站交互自主完成在线任务，但它们暴露于开放网络环境使得它们容易受到嵌入在HTML内容或视觉界面中的提示注入攻击。现有的防护模型仍然存在以下问题：对未见过的领域和攻击模式的泛化能力有限，对良性内容的误报率高，由于每一步增加的延迟导致部署效率降低，以及容易受到随时间演变或直接针对防护模型本身的对抗性攻击。为了解决这些限制，我们提出了WARD（Web代理鲁棒防御提示注入），一个用于安全高效Web代理的实用防护模型。WARD构建于WARD-Base（一个包含约17.7万个样本的大型数据集，来自719个高流量URL和平台）和WARD-PIG（一个专门设计用于针对防护模型的提示注入攻击的数据集）之上。我们进一步引入了A3T，一种自适应对抗性攻击训练框架，通过基于记忆的攻击者和防护共同进化过程迭代地增强WARD。大量实验表明，WARD在分布外基准测试上实现了近乎完美的召回率，保持低误报率以保留代理效用，在显著分布偏移下对针对防护模型和自适应攻击保持鲁棒性，并且与代理并行高效运行而不引入额外延迟。

Original abstract: Web agents can autonomously complete online tasks by interacting with websites, but their exposure to open web environments makes them vulnerable to prompt injection attacks embedded in HTML content or visual interfaces. Existing guard models still suffer from limited generalization to unseen domains and attack patterns, high false positive rates on benign content, reduced deployment efficiency due to added latency at each step, and vulnerability to adversarial attacks that evolve over time or directly target the guard itself. To address these limitations, we propose WARD (Web Agent Robust Defense against Prompt Injection), a practical guard model for secure and efficient web agents. WARD is built on WARD-Base, a large-scale dataset with around 177K samples collected from 719 high-traffic URLs and platforms, and WARD-PIG, a dedicated dataset designed for prompt injection attacks targeting the guard model. We further introduce A3T, an adaptive adversarial attack training framework that iteratively strengthens WARD through a memory-based attacker and guard co-evolution process. Extensive experiments show that WARD achieves nearly perfect recall on out-of-distribution benchmarks, maintains low false positive rates to preserve agent utility, remains robust against guard-targeted and adaptive attacks under substantial distribution shifts, and runs efficiently in parallel with the agent without introducing additional latency.

### [80] [Autonomous Intelligent Agents for Natural-Language-Driven Web Execution with Integrated Security Assurance](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15281v1)
*Vinil Pasupuleti,Siva Rama Krishna Varma Bayyavarapu,Shrey Tyagi*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代Web测试套件容易因UI重构、时序变化等问题失效，导致开发人员放弃，需要一种更可靠的自动化测试方法。

Method: 采用AI驱动框架，集成导航可靠性、上下文感知选择器生成、生成后验证、智能等待注入和失败学习五种策略，基于容器化工作节点架构（解耦编排与浏览器执行），并支持自然语言驱动的安全测试。

Result: 在四个生产应用和176个场景中，脚本生成成功率从55%提升至93%，导航失败减少8倍，消除80%时序竞态条件，测试创建时间减少75%；安全测试检测85%身份认证绕过和95%输入验证缺陷，误报率低于12%。

Conclusion: 该框架有效解决了Web测试套件失效问题，并首次提出自然语言驱动的安全测试，为自动化测试领域做出新颖贡献。

中文摘要：现代Web测试套件容易失效。UI重构破坏了定位器，时间变化导致竞态条件，几周内开发人员就彻底放弃了整个套件。本文提出了一种AI驱动的自主测试框架，通过五种集成策略——导航可靠性、上下文感知选择器生成、生成后验证、智能等待注入和失败学习——来解决这些失效模式。该框架基于容器化的工作节点架构实现，将编排与长时间运行的浏览器执行解耦。在四个生产应用程序和176个场景中进行的评估显示，该框架将脚本生成成功率从55%提高到93%，导航失败减少了8倍，消除了80%的与时间相关的竞态条件，并将测试创建时间比手动Selenium编写减少了75%。该框架自然延伸至安全验证：测试人员用通俗英语描述攻击场景——“尝试访问另一个用户的发票”——代理将其转换为与OWASP十大威胁对齐的浏览器探测，检测到85%的身份验证绕过漏洞和95%的输入验证缺陷，误报率低于12%。据我们所知，这种自然语言驱动的安全测试是对该领域的一个新颖贡献。

Original abstract: Modern web test suites rot. A UI refactor breaks locators, a timing change causes race conditions, and within weeks developers abandon the suite entirely. This paper presents an AI-driven autonomous testing framework that addresses these failure modes through five integrated strategies - navigation reliability, context-aware selector generation, post-generation validation, smart wait injection, and failure learning - implemented over a containerised worker architecture that decouples orchestration from long-running browser execution. Evaluated across four production applications and 176 scenarios, the framework improves script generation success from 55% to 93%, achieves an 8x reduction in navigation failures, eliminates 80% of timing-related race conditions, and reduces test creation time by 75% compared to manual Selenium authoring. The framework extends naturally to security validation: testers describe attack scenarios in plain English - "try accessing another user's invoice" - which the agent converts to OWASP Top 10-aligned browser probes, detecting 85% of authentication bypass vulnerabilities and 95% of input validation flaws with false positive rates below 12%. Natural-language-driven security testing of this kind represents, to our knowledge, a novel contribution to the field.

</details>


### [81] [Hidden in Memory: Sleeper Memory Poisoning in LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15338v2)
*Sidharth Pulipaka,Stanislau Hlebik,Leonidas Raghav,Sahar Abdelnabi,Vyas Raina,Ivaxi Sheth,Mario Fritz*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: LLM agent记忆投毒攻击，涉及agent安全与可靠性。

TL;DR: 提出睡眠记忆投毒攻击，利用LLM持久记忆注入虚假信息，在多个会话后仍可操纵模型行为，攻击成功率高达99.8%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 持久记忆使LLM能够跨会话存储用户信息，但这也为攻击者提供了长期攻击面，现有研究未充分探索此类延迟攻击。

Method: 设计睡眠记忆投毒攻击：在外部上下文中嵌入恶意内容，当LLM处理时将其写入持久记忆；随后在后续对话中通过检索触发，引导模型执行攻击者意图的动作。

Result: 在GPT-5.5和Kimi-K2.6上，中毒记忆写入成功率分别达99.8%和95%；成功检索后，60-89%的评估中模型执行了攻击者意图的智能体行为。

Conclusion: 持久记忆作为长期攻击面具有严重安全风险，需防御措施防止记忆被恶意篡改和利用。

中文摘要：大型语言模型越来越多地配备持久记忆，使得助手能够在不同会话中存储用户特定信息以实现个性化和连续性。这种状态性引入了一种新的安全风险：对抗性内容可能破坏助手的记忆，从而影响未来的交互。我们提出并研究了睡眠记忆投毒，这是一种延迟攻击，攻击者操纵外部上下文（如文档、网页或仓库），使助手存储关于用户的虚构记忆。与传统的提示注入不同，该攻击可以保持休眠状态，并在后续多次对话中重新出现。我们评估了完整的攻击流程：中毒记忆是否被写入、后续是否被检索，以及最终是否被用来引导后续对话。在多个状态化LLM助手中，中毒记忆在GPT-5.5上的添加成功率达99.8%，在Kimi-K2.6上达95%。关键在于，在成功检索中，中毒记忆导致攻击者意图的智能体行为在模型评估中占60-89%。这些结果表明，持久记忆可以作为跨越多个未来对话的长期攻击面。

Original abstract: Large language models are increasingly augmented with persistent memory, allowing assistants to store user-specific information across sessions for personalization and continuity. This statefulness introduces a new security risk: adversarial content can corrupt what an assistant remembers and thereby influence future interactions. We propose and study sleeper memory poisoning, a delayed attack in which an adversary manipulates external context, such as a document, webpage, or repository, to cause the assistant to store a fabricated memory about the user. Unlike conventional prompt injection, the attack can remain dormant and re-emerge across multiple later conversations. We evaluate the full attack pipeline: whether poisoned memories are written, later retrieved, and ultimately used to steer the following conversations. Across stateful LLM assistants, poisoned memories were added up to 99.8% on GPT-5.5 and 95% on Kimi-K2.6. Crucially, among successful retrievals, poisoned memories cause attacker-intended agentic actions in 60-89% of evaluations across models. These results show that persistent memory can act as a long-term attack surface across multiple future conversations.

</details>


### [82] [The End of Trust: How Agentic AI Breaks Security Assumptions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16436v1)
*Osama Zafar,Alexander Nemecek,Erman Ayday*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 讨论agentic AI的安全范式，涉及agent可靠性与安全控制，可启发agent安全设计。

TL;DR: 代理型人工智能打破了欺骗的保真度与规模之间的权衡，引入了'无限冒充者'攻击模型，并需要转向'默认怀疑'范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统安全范式依赖于攻击者在欺骗逼真度和规模之间的经济权衡；代理型人工智能消除了这一权衡，导致现有防御机制失效。

Method: 我们提出了'无限冒充者'攻击模型，其中自主代理劫持已有信任关系，并提出了'默认怀疑'范式，将安全重心从认证行为者转向评估行为。

Result: 检测型防御因合成输出与真实输出无法区分而失效；安全范式被耗尽。

Conclusion: 安全必须从认证行为者转向评估行为，且当平台成为监管基础时会产生治理张力。

中文摘要：数十年来，数字交互的安全性一直依赖于一个未被承认的经济约束。攻击者在欺骗的逼真度和可部署规模之间面临权衡。令人信服的冒充需要持续的人力投入，且局限于少数高价值目标，而大规模攻击则牺牲可信度以换取覆盖面。检测系统、验证机制和用户安全意识培训都隐式地针对这种权衡所产生的廉价欺骗痕迹进行了校准。代理型人工智能打破了这一权衡，使得大规模生产高保真、个性化定制的欺骗成为可能。我们认为，这一转变并非仅仅加剧了威胁格局，而是耗尽了一种安全范式。我们引入了“无限冒充者”攻击模型，其中自主代理插入两个已有信任关系的双方之间，劫持现有关系而非从头建立。面向检测的防御措施共同假设生成式进展正在消除的一个前提——合成输出与真实输出是可区分的。我们提出了一种“默认怀疑”范式，将安全从认证行为者转向评估行为，并考察了当平台成为数字交互的监管基础时所产生的治理张力。

Original abstract: For decades, the security of digital interaction has rested on an unacknowledged economic constraint. Attackers faced a tradeoff between the fidelity of a deception and the scale at which it could be deployed. Convincing impersonation required sustained human effort and was confined to a narrow set of high-value targets, while mass-market attacks sacrificed plausibility for reach. Detection systems, verification mechanisms, and user awareness training have all been implicitly calibrated to the artifacts of cheap deception that this tradeoff produced. Agentic AI collapses the tradeoff, allowing high-fidelity, individually tailored deception to be produced at mass-market scale. We argue that this shift exhausts a security paradigm rather than merely intensifying the threat landscape. We introduce the Infinite Impostor, an attack model in which an autonomous agent interposes itself between two parties who already trust each other, hijacking an existing relationship rather than building a new one from scratch. Detection-oriented defenses share an assumption that generative progress is eliminating, that synthetic outputs are distinguishable from authentic ones. We propose a suspect-by-default paradigm that shifts security from authenticating actors to evaluating actions, and examine the governance tensions that arise when platforms become the regulatory substrate of digital interaction.

</details>

### [83] [ATLAS: Agentic or Latent Visual Reasoning? One Word is Enough for Both](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15198v1)
*Ziyu Guo,Rain Liu,Xinyan Chen,Pheng-Ann Heng*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 提出功能性token结合agentic和潜在推理，可迁移至coding agent中的工具调用与推理。

TL;DR: 提出ATLAS框架，使用功能标记整合代理操作和潜在视觉推理，避免中间图像生成，兼容标准训练，并引入LA-GRPO稳定强化学习，在视觉推理基准上表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉推理方法（直接生成图像、代理推理、潜在推理）各有优缺点：直接生成计算昂贵，代理推理有延迟，潜在推理泛化差且训练困难。因此需结合两者优势，提出高效且兼容的框架。

Method: ATLAS框架：每个功能标记对应一个内化的视觉操作，作为标准token通过下一个标记预测生成，无需视觉监督。同时引入LA-GRPO，通过静态加权辅助目标锚定功能标记，解决RL中标记稀疏性问题。

Result: 在多个具有挑战性的视觉推理基准上，ATLAS取得优越性能，且保持清晰的可解释性。

Conclusion: ATLAS提供了一种结合代理操作和潜在推理的新范式，有望推动未来视觉推理研究。

中文摘要：视觉推理常常与中间视觉状态交织在一起，已成为该领域一个有前景的方向。一种直接的方法是在推理过程中通过统一模型直接生成图像，但这种方法计算成本高且架构复杂。最近的替代方案包括通过代码或工具调用的代理推理，以及使用可学习隐藏嵌入的潜在推理。然而，代理方法因外部执行而带来上下文切换延迟，而潜在方法缺乏任务泛化能力且难以通过自回归并行化进行训练。为了结合它们的优势同时减轻其局限性，我们提出了ATLAS框架，其中单个离散的“词”（称为功能标记）既充当代理操作，又充当潜在视觉推理单元。每个功能标记与一个内化的视觉操作相关联，但不需要视觉监督，并且仍然是分词器词汇表中的标准标记，可以通过下一个标记预测生成。这种设计避免了冗长的中间视觉内容生成，同时保持了与普通可扩展SFT和RL训练的兼容性，无需架构或方法上的修改。为了进一步解决RL中功能标记的稀疏性问题，我们引入了潜在锚定GRPO（LA-GRPO），通过静态加权的辅助目标来锚定功能标记，从而稳定训练并提供更强的梯度更新。大量实验和分析表明，ATLAS在具有挑战性的基准测试上取得了优越的性能，同时保持了清晰的可解释性。我们希望ATLAS能为未来的视觉推理研究提供一种新范式。

Original abstract: Visual reasoning, often interleaved with intermediate visual states, has emerged as a promising direction in the field. A straightforward approach is to directly generate images via unified models during reasoning, but this is computationally expensive and architecturally non-trivial. Recent alternatives include agentic reasoning through code or tool calls, and latent reasoning with learnable hidden embeddings. However, agentic methods incur context-switching latency from external execution, while latent methods lack task generalization and are difficult to train with autoregressive parallelization. To combine their strengths while mitigating their limitations, we propose ATLAS, a framework in which a single discrete 'word', termed as a functional token, serves both as an agentic operation and a latent visual reasoning unit. Each functional token is associated with an internalized visual operation, yet requires no visual supervision and remains a standard token in the tokenizer vocabulary, which can be generated via next-token prediction. This design avoids verbose intermediate visual content generation, while preserving compatibility with the vanilla scalable SFT and RL training, without architectural or methodological modifications. To further address the sparsity of functional tokens during RL, we introduce Latent-Anchored GRPO (LA-GRPO), which stabilizes the training by anchoring functional tokens with a statically weighted auxiliary objective, providing stronger gradient updates. Extensive experiments and analyses demonstrate that ATLAS achieves superior performance on challenging benchmarks while maintaining clear interpretability. We hope ATLAS offers a new paradigm inspiring future visual reasoning research.

</details>

# cs.OS [[Back]](#toc)

### [84] [TuxBot: Semantic-Aware Online OS Tuning with Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15026v2)
*Georgios Liargkovas,Mihir Nitin Joshi,Hubertus Franke,Kostis Kaffes*

Main category: cs.OS

Selection reason: LLM驱动的OS调优，直接类比代码性能优化

TL;DR: TuxBot是一个基于语言模型指导的主机端操作系统调优框架，通过紧凑决策上下文和双层循环机制，在13个实时工作负载上显著提升性能并避免退化区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有控制器与实时主机不匹配，忽略跨旋钮策略结构，在应用指标不可用时失效，且可能导致持久退化。

Method: TuxBot将旋钮模式、遥测、配置、历史等转化为紧凑决策上下文，使用快速循环和慢速循环，所有更改经过类型验证，利用语言模型指导。

Result: 在13个工作负载上，稳定阶段性能提升72.5%和153.3%，30窗口成本0.20美元，仅用主机指标比基线高93.7个百分点，避免退化区域。

Conclusion: TuxBot有效实现稳态OS调优，低成本高收益，避免了结构盲目探索的退化问题。

中文摘要：在线操作系统调优可以改善长时间运行的服务，但现有的控制器与实时主机匹配不佳。它们将调度器、电源、内存和I/O控制视为黑箱变量，并优化标量奖励。这种观点忽略了跨旋钮策略结构，在应用程序指标不可用时失效，并且可能将运行中的服务送入退化区域，即使在移除不良设置后仍持续存在。我们提出了TuxBot，一个带有有界语言模型指导的主机端稳态操作系统调优框架。TuxBot将旋钮模式、遥测、当前配置、最近的行动-响应历史以及检索到的先前运行记录转化为紧凑的决策上下文。一个快速循环提出低延迟更新，一个较慢循环定期修订搜索策略，每个提议的更改在到达内核或sysctl接口之前都经过类型验证。这使得控制器能够推理操作系统控制含义和间接性能信号，同时保持模型成本、延迟和权限受限。我们在来自五个基准套件的13个实时工作负载上评估TuxBot，同时调整多达41个Linux参数。在整个套件中，TuxBot将稳定阶段性能比默认设置提高了72.5%，相对于最强的非LLM基线提高了153.3%。一个30窗口会话的模型调用成本约为0.20美元。仅使用主机级指标，TuxBot仍然比给定直接应用目标的基线高出93.7个百分点，同时避免了结构盲目探索所达到的严重退化区域。

Original abstract: Online OS tuning can improve long-running services, but existing controllers are poorly matched to live hosts. They treat scheduler, power, memory, and I/O controls as black-box variables and optimize a scalar reward. This view ignores cross-knob policy structure, breaks down when application metrics are unavailable, and can send a running service into degraded regions that persist after the bad setting is removed. We present TuxBot, a host-side framework for steady-state OS tuning with bounded language-model guidance. TuxBot turns knob schemas, telemetry, current configuration, recent action--response history, and retrieved prior runs into a compact decision context. A fast loop proposes low-latency updates, a slower loop periodically revises the search strategy, and every proposed change passes through typed validation before reaching kernel or sysctl interfaces. This lets the controller reason about OS-control meaning and indirect performance signals while keeping model cost, latency, and authority constrained. We evaluate TuxBot on 13 live workloads from five benchmark suites while tuning up to 41 Linux parameters. Across the suite, TuxBot improves stable-phase performance by 72.5% over default settings and by 153.3% relative to the strongest non-LLM baseline. A 30-window session costs about $0.20 in model calls. With only host-level metrics, TuxBot still outperforms baselines given direct application objectives by 93.7 percentage points, while avoiding severe degraded regions reached by structure-blind exploration.

</details>

# cs.CE [[Back]](#toc)

### [85] [From Feedback Loops to Policy Updates: Reinforcement Fine-Tuning for LLM-Based Alpha Factor Discovery](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15412v1)
*Lingzhe Zhang,Tong Jia,Yunpeng Zhai,Zixuan Xie,Chiming Duan,Minghua He,Philip S. Yu,Ying Li*

Main category: cs.CE

Selection reason: 强化微调自动因子发现，RL fine-tuning方法可迁移至代码优化agent。

TL;DR: 提出QuantEvolver，一种基于强化微调的自进化Alpha因子发现框架，通过将评估转化为策略更新避免上下文爆炸，生成更高质量和互补的因子池。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM因子发现方法依赖提示级别的反馈循环，导致上下文爆炸、成本增加、信息稀释和搜索停滞；且大LLM的稳定偏好导致冗余和结构相似。

Method: QuantEvolver通过强化微调，利用种子因子和多样训练任务生成因子DSL，经制度回测评估后，用多样性-互补性奖励更新Miner LLM参数，积累高质量因子到数据库。

Result: 在三个真实市场基准上，QuantEvolver在每个任务的主要评估指标上持续优于现有LLM基线，产生更高质量和更互补的因子池。

Conclusion: QuantEvolver有效解决了现有方法的上下文爆炸和搜索停滞问题，提升了因子发现的质量和多样性。

中文摘要：现代量化交易越来越依赖系统化模型从大规模金融数据中提取预测信号，其中Alpha因子发现是将市场观察转化为可交易信号的核心环节。近期基于LLM的方法在自动化因子生成方面展现出潜力，但大多数方法仍依赖于提示级别的生成-评估-反馈循环进行迭代优化。随着循环变长，反复追加的历史候选和反馈会导致上下文爆炸、增加推理成本、稀释有用信息并引入反馈漂移。此外，这些方法通常依赖非常大的LLM，其稳定的生成偏好可能导致结构相似的表达式、冗余的候选和搜索停滞。为解决这些局限性，我们提出\textsc{QuantEvolver}——一种基于强化微调的自进化Alpha因子发现框架。\textsc{QuantEvolver}不将反馈累积在提示中，而是将可执行的量化评估转化为策略更新，使Miner LLM通过参数学习内化历史优化经验。具体而言，\textsc{QuantEvolver}构建高质量种子因子，构建多样化的种子-时间窗口训练任务，生成可执行的因子DSL表达式，通过制度回测评估它们，并使用多样性-互补性奖励优化Miner LLM。训练过程中，高质量因子持续累积到挖掘因子数据库中，该库作为最终发现的因子库。在三个真实市场基准上的大量实验证明了\textsc{QuantEvolver}的有效性，它在每个任务的主要评估指标上持续优于现有基于LLM的Alpha因子发现基线，并产生更高质量和更互补的因子池。

Original abstract: Modern quantitative trading increasingly relies on systematic models to extract predictive signals from large-scale financial data, where alpha factor discovery plays a central role in transforming market observations into tradable signals. Recent LLM-based methods have shown promise in automating factor generation, but most of them still rely on prompt-level generation--evaluation--feedback loops for iterative optimization. As the loop becomes longer, repeatedly appended historical candidates and feedback can cause context explosion, increase inference cost, dilute useful information, and introduce feedback drift. Moreover, these methods often depend on very large LLMs whose stable generation preferences may lead to structurally similar expressions, redundant candidates, and search stagnation. To address these limitations, we propose \textsc{QuantEvolver}, a self-evolving alpha factor discovery framework based on reinforcement fine-tuning. Instead of accumulating feedback in the prompt, \textsc{QuantEvolver} converts executable quantitative evaluation into policy updates, enabling a Miner LLM to internalize historical optimization experience through parameter learning. Specifically, \textsc{QuantEvolver} constructs high-quality seed factors, builds diverse seed--time-window training tasks, generates executable Factor DSL expressions, evaluates them through Regime Backtest, and optimizes the Miner LLM with Diversity-Complementarity Reward. During training, high-quality factors are continuously accumulated in a Mined Factor Database, which serves as the final discovered factor library. Extensive experiments on three realistic market benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness of \textsc{QuantEvolver}, which consistently improves the primary evaluation metric of each task over existing LLM-based alpha factor discovery baselines, produces higher-quality and more complementary factor pools.

</details>

### [86] [Agentic Design of Compositional Descriptors via Autoresearch for Materials Science Applications](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14671v1)
*Matteo Cobelli,Stefano Sanvito*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

Selection reason: 基于LLM coding agent的自动研究框架，迭代设计特征，可迁移到agent驱动的代码优化

TL;DR: 本文提出Automat自动化研究框架，利用大语言模型代理自动设计材料描述符，在带隙和居里温度预测任务中优于基线，同时保持化学可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测试自动化研究代理能否在模型选择和超参数优化之外执行描述符设计这一高层次科学任务，减少手动特征工程。

Method: 基于大语言模型的编码代理在自动化研究框架中迭代生成仅成分的描述符，通过随机森林工作流评估，并使用OpenAI Codex（GPT-5.5）实现。

Result: 在带隙和居里温度预测中，Automat生成的任务特定描述符族优于多种基线，且化学可解释，但存在冗余、对贪婪特征扩展敏感等问题。

Conclusion: 自动化研究代理能自动生成竞争性材料描述符，但需改进搜索策略和复杂度控制以克服当前局限。

中文摘要：自动化研究提供了一种灵活的科学任务自动化范式，其中AI代理针对定量目标提出、实施、评估并完善候选解决方案。在此，我们使用基于成分的材料性质预测来测试此类代理是否能执行超出模型选择和超参数优化的任务：输入描述符的设计。我们引入了Automat，一种自动化研究框架，其中基于大语言模型的编码代理为化学化合物生成仅成分的描述符，并使用随机森林工作流程进行评估。该代理仅限于从化学式中可推导的信息，并迭代地提出、实施和测试化学驱动的描述符策略。我们将Automat（使用OpenAI Codex和GPT-5.5作为编码代理）应用于无机材料实验带隙和铁磁化合物居里温度的预测。在这两项任务中，Automat均优于分数成分、Magpie以及分数成分/Magpie组合基线，同时产生化学可解释的描述符族。这些结果证明，自动化研究代理可以在运行期间无需手动特征工程的情况下生成具有竞争性的任务特定材料描述符。它们也揭示了当前局限性，包括描述符冗余、对贪婪特征扩展的敏感性，以及需要显式的复杂性控制、描述符剪枝和更复杂的搜索策略。

Original abstract: Autoresearch offers a flexible paradigm for automating scientific tasks, in which an AI agent proposes, implements, evaluates, and refines candidate solutions against a quantitative objective. Here, we use composition-based materials-property prediction to test whether such agents can perform a task beyond model selection and hyperparameter optimization: the design of input descriptors. We introduce Automat, an autoresearch framework where a coding agent based on a large language model generates composition-only descriptors for chemical compounds and evaluates them using a random forest workflow. The agent is restricted to information derivable from chemical formulas and iteratively proposes, implements, and tests chemically motivated descriptor strategies. We apply Automat, with OpenAI Codex using GPT-5.5 as the coding agent, to the prediction of experimental band gaps in inorganic materials and Curie temperatures in ferromagnetic compounds. In both tasks, Automat improves over fractional-composition, Magpie, and combined fractional-composition/Magpie baselines, while producing descriptor families that are chemically interpretable. These results provide a demonstration that autoresearch agents can generate competitive, task-specific materials descriptors without manual feature engineering during the run. They also reveal current limitations, including descriptor redundancy, sensitivity to greedy feature expansion, and the need for explicit complexity control, descriptor pruning, and more sophisticated search strategies.

### [87] [Agentic Recommender System with Hierarchical Belief-State Memory](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14401v2)
*Xiang Shen,Yuhang Zhou,Yifan Wu,Zhuokai Zhao,Siyu Lin,Lei Huang,Qianqian Zhong,Lizhu Zhang,Benyu Zhang,Xiangjun Fan,Hong Yan*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 记忆增强推荐agent，通用记忆管理架构可迁移。

TL;DR: 提出MARS框架，通过三级记忆结构和LLM调度的六操作生命周期，将推荐转化为部分可观察问题，显著提升推荐性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆增强的LLM代理在个性化推荐中使用扁平记忆表示，无法区分短暂信号与稳定偏好，且缺乏记忆演变的完整生命周期管理。

Method: 将推荐视为部分可观察问题，维护包含事件记忆、偏好记忆和概要记忆的三级结构化信念状态，并通过LLM计划器自适应调度提取、强化、弱化、巩固、遗忘和再合成六种操作。

Result: 在四个InstructRec基准上，HR@1平均提升26.4%，NDCG@10平均提升10.3%，在动态场景下代理调度带来进一步增益。

Conclusion: MARS通过结构化记忆和智能生命周期管理，有效提升了推荐系统的准确性和适应性，证明了代理调度在记忆演化中的优势。

中文摘要：记忆增强的LLM代理已经推进了个性化推荐，然而现有方法普遍采用扁平的记忆表示，将短暂的信号与稳定的偏好混为一谈，并且没有提供完整的生命周期来管理记忆应如何演变。我们提出了MARS（记忆增强的代理推荐系统），一个将推荐视为部分可观察问题并维护结构化信念状态的框架，该状态逐步将噪声的行为观察抽象为用户偏好的紧凑估计。MARS将这种信念状态组织成三个层级：事件记忆缓冲原始信号，偏好记忆维护具有明确强度和证据追踪的细粒度可变块，概要记忆将所有偏好提炼成连贯的自然语言叙述。一个完整的六种操作生命周期——提取、强化、弱化、巩固、遗忘和再合成——由基于LLM的计划器自适应调度，而不是固定间隔的启发式方法。在四个InstructRec基准领域的实验表明，MARS实现了最先进的性能，在HR@1上平均提升了26.4%，在NDCG@10上平均提升了10.3%，超过了最强的基线，并且在不断变化的环境中通过代理调度获得了进一步的改进。

Original abstract: Memory-augmented LLM agents have advanced personalized recommendation, yet existing approaches universally adopt flat memory representations that conflate ephemeral signals with stable preferences, and none provides a complete lifecycle governing how memory should evolve. We propose MARS (Memory-Augmented Agentic Recommender System), a framework that treats recommendation as a partially observable problem and maintains a structured belief state that progressively abstracts noisy behavioral observations into a compact estimate of user preferences. MARS organizes this belief state into three tiers: event memory buffers raw signals, preference memory maintains fine-grained mutable chunks with explicit strength and evidence tracking, and profile memory distills all preferences into a coherent natural language narrative. A complete lifecycle of six operations -- extraction, reinforcement, weakening, consolidation, forgetting, and resynthesis -- is adaptively scheduled by an LLM-based planner rather than fixed-interval heuristics. Experiments on four InstructRec benchmark domains show that MARS achieves state-of-the-art performance with average improvements of 26.4% in HR@1 and 10.3% in NDCG@10 over the strongest baselines with further gains from agentic scheduling in evolving settings.

</details>


### [88] [Does RAG Know When Retrieval Is Wrong? Diagnosing Context Compliance under Knowledge Conflict](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14473v3)
*Yihang Chen,Pin Qian,Su Wang,Sipeng Zhang,Huan Xu,Shuhuai Lin,Xinpeng Wei*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 诊断RAG中上下文遵从问题，提出干预机制，对agent检索与推理有启发。

TL;DR: 提出Context-Driven Decomposition (CDD) 方法，通过信念分解探测和干预检索增强生成中的上下文遵从问题，在多个基准上验证了三种模式，表明CDD能有效提升对抗鲁棒性并揭示模型间机制差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG中上下文遵从问题难以通过准确率揭示检索上下文对答案的因果影响，需要一种能在推理时探测和干预冲突的新方法。

Method: 引入CDD，一种推理时的信念分解探针，通过分解模型对检索上下文和自身知识的信念来测量和干预上下文遵从，作为受控检索冲突的干预机制。

Result: P1：标准RAG在TruthfulQA误解注入上准确率仅15.0%；P2：CDD在Gemini-2.5-Flash上因果敏感性达64.1%，而Claude变体在[-3%,+7%]内；P3：CDD在Epi-Scale上对时间偏移达71.3%，干扰证据达69.9%。

Conclusion: 上下文遵从性是标准RAG可探测和干预的结构轴，与检索质量和单一鲁棒性不同，CDD有效暴露并缓解了该问题，并推动Epi-Scale基准的发布以支持系统研究。

中文摘要：检索增强生成（RAG）中的上下文遵从机制发生在检索到的上下文主导最终答案时，即使它与模型的参数知识相冲突。仅凭准确率并不能揭示在此类冲突下检索到的上下文如何因果性地影响答案。我们引入了上下文驱动分解（CDD），这是一种在推理时运行的信念分解探针，并作为受控检索冲突的干预机制。通过Epi-Scale压力测试、TruthfulQA误解注入和跨模型复现，CDD揭示了三种模式。P1：上下文遵从性可以在上界对抗性设置中测量，其中标准RAG在TruthfulQA误解注入（N=500）上达到15.0%的准确率。P2：对抗性准确率的提升跨模型族迁移——CDD提高了Gemini-2.5-Flash和Claude Haiku/Sonnet/Opus上的准确率——但理由-答案的因果耦合并不迁移。CDD在Gemini-2.5-Flash上达到64.1%的误解注入因果敏感性，而所有三种Claude变体的敏感性落在[-3%, +7%]范围内，表明Claude侧的准确率提升通过一种与显式冲突解决轨迹不同的机制运作。P3：显式冲突分解提高了在时间漂移和噪声干扰下的鲁棒性，CDD在完整的Epi-Scale对抗性基准上，对时间偏移达到71.3%，对干扰证据达到69.9%。这三种模式将上下文遵从性识别为一个结构轴，沿着该轴可以对标准RAG进行探测和干预，这不同于检索质量或单一方法鲁棒性问题，并促使发布Epi-Scale以进行跨模型族和检索管道的系统研究。

Original abstract: The Context-Compliance Regime in Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) occurs when retrieved context dominates the final answer even when it conflicts with the model's parametric knowledge. Accuracy alone does not reveal how retrieved context causally shapes answers under such conflict. We introduce Context-Driven Decomposition (CDD), a belief-decomposition probe that operates at inference time and serves as an intervention mechanism for controlled retrieval conflict. Across Epi-Scale stress tests, TruthfulQA misconception injection, and cross-model reruns, CDD exposes three patterns. P1: context compliance is measurable in an upper-bound adversarial setting, where Standard RAG reaches 15.0% accuracy on TruthfulQA misconception injection (N=500). P2: adversarial accuracy gains transfer across model families -- CDD improves accuracy on Gemini-2.5-Flash and on Claude Haiku/Sonnet/Opus -- but rationale-answer causal coupling does not transfer. CDD reaches 64.1% mistake-injection causal sensitivity on Gemini-2.5-Flash, while sensitivities for all three Claude variants fall in the [-3%, +7%] range, suggesting that the Claude-side accuracy gains operate through a mechanism distinct from the explicit conflict-resolution trace. P3: explicit conflict decomposition improves robustness under temporal drift and noisy distractors, with CDD reaching 71.3% on temporal shifts and 69.9% on distractor evidence on the full Epi-Scale adversarial benchmark. These three patterns identify context-compliance as a structural axis along which standard RAG can be probed and intervened on, distinct from retrieval-quality or single-method robustness questions, and motivate releasing Epi-Scale for systematic study across model families and retrieval pipelines.

</details>


### [89] [Dimension-Level Intent Fidelity Evaluation for Large Language Models: Evidence from Structured Prompt Ablation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14517v1)
*GAng Peng*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: LLM输出意图忠实度评估框架，对Agent输出可靠性评估有潜在启发

TL;DR: 提出维度级意图保真度评估框架，发现整体评分无法区分结构恢复与意图保真度，且存在系统性分裂，维度分数更可靠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 整体评估分数无法区分模型是否再现结构形式与保留用户意图，需要更细粒度的评估方法。

Method: 通过结构化提示消融研究，在2880个输出上分别测量每个语义维度的结构恢复和意图保真度，并进行了人类评估、公-私分解、代理注释和权重扰动实验。

Result: 发现中文输出中25.7%、英文输出中58.6%存在完美整体评分但维度意图缺陷；维度保真度分数更符合人类判断；中等不对齐可被吸收，严重反转有害。

Conclusion: 维度级意图保真度评估是整体评估的必要补充，用于评估面向用户特定任务的LLM输出。

中文摘要：整体评估分数能够捕捉输出整体质量，但无法区分模型是否再现了用户请求的结构形式与是否保留了用户的特定意图。我们提出了一种维度级意图保真度评估框架，通过结构化提示消融研究应用于2880个输出，涵盖三种语言、三个任务领域和六个大型语言模型，分别独立测量每个语义维度的结构恢复和意图保真度。该框架揭示了一种系统的结构-保真度分裂：在具有完整配对分数的中文输出中，25.7%获得了完美的整体对齐分数（GA=5），同时表现出可测量的维度意图缺陷；在英文输出中，这一比例上升至58.6%。人工评估确认这些分裂区输出代表了真正的质量缺陷，并且维度保真度分数比整体分数更可靠地跟踪人类判断。对2520个消融单元的公私分解刻画了模型何时成功补偿缺失意图以及何时失败，而代理注释则区分了先验可推断性与默认可恢复性。权重扰动实验表明，中等程度的不对齐通常被吸收，而严重的维度反转则始终有害。这些发现表明，在评估面向用户特定任务的LLM输出时，维度级意图保真度评估是整体评估的必要补充。

Original abstract: Holistic evaluation scores capture overall output quality but do not distinguish whether a model reproduced the structural form of a user's request from whether it preserved the user's specific intent. We propose a dimension-level intent fidelity evaluation framework, applied here through a structured prompt ablation study across 2,880 outputs spanning three languages, three task domains, and six LLMs, that separately measures structural recovery and intent fidelity for each semantic dimension. This framework reveals a systematic structural-fidelity split: among Chinese-language outputs with complete paired scores, 25.7% received perfect holistic alignment scores (GA=5) while exhibiting measurable dimensional intent deficits; among English-language outputs, this proportion rose to 58.6%. Human evaluation confirmed that these split-zone outputs represent genuine quality deficits and that dimensional fidelity scores track human judgements more reliably than holistic scores do. A public-private decomposition of 2,520 ablation cells characterises when models successfully compensate for missing intent and when they fail, while proxy annotation distinguishes prior inferability from default recoverability. A weight-perturbation experiment shows that moderate misalignment is typically absorbed, whereas severe dimensional inversion is consistently harmful. These findings demonstrate that dimension-level intent fidelity evaluation is a necessary complement to holistic assessment when evaluating LLM outputs for user-specific tasks.

</details>


### [90] [Mechanical Enforcement for LLM Governance:Evidence of Governance-Task Decoupling in Financial Decision Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14744v1)
*José Manuel de la Chica Rodríguez,Carlos Martí-González*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 探讨LLM治理的机械执行，对agent安全控制有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 在受监管金融工作流中，机械执行比纯文本治理更有效地确保LLM策略合规，显著提升治理指标和任务准确性，且治理与任务性能解耦。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在受监管金融工作流中受自然语言策略约束，存在委托-代理失败，现有评估只衡量任务准确性而不衡量决策理由层面的治理合规性，因此需要新的治理指标和更有效的执行机制。

Method: 引入五个治理指标量化理由层面的策略合规性，在合成银行领域比较纯文本治理与四种机械执行原语，使用因果消融验证每个原语的必要性。

Result: 纯文本治理下27%的延迟决策无信息；机械执行将此比率降低73%，延迟决策信息内容翻倍，任务准确性从MCC 0.43提升至0.88，且改进源于架构分离，机械执行在结构压力下保持治理质量而任务性能下降。

Conclusion: 治理和任务评估是独立维度，准确性不能作为治理的充分代理；机械执行通过架构分离显著提升治理合规性，且每个原语单独必要。

中文摘要：在受监管的金融工作流中，大语言模型受到同一模型解释的自然语言策略的约束，这导致了委托-代理失败：输出可能看似合规但实际上并不合规。现有的评估衡量任务准确性，但不衡量治理是否在决策理由层面约束了行为——而受监管的决策必须可审计。我们引入了五个治理指标，在理由层面量化策略合规性，并在一个合成银行领域中将其应用于比较纯文本治理与机械执行：四种在模型解释循环之外运行的原语。在纯文本治理下，27%的延迟决策不包含任何决策相关信息。机械执行将此比率降低了73%，使延迟决策的信息内容增加了一倍以上，并将任务准确性从MCC~0.43提高到0.88。改进源于架构分离：在机械执行下，LLM生成的理由与纯文本治理显示出可比的CDL——收益来自于将明确决策从模型控制中移除。因果消融证实每个原语都是单独必要的。我们的核心发现是治理-任务解耦：在结构压力下，纯文本治理在两个维度上同时退化，而机械执行即使在任务性能下降时也能保持治理质量。这意味着治理和任务评估是不同的维度：准确性不能作为受监管AI系统中治理的充分代理。

Original abstract: Large language models in regulated financial workflows are governed by natural-language policies that the same model interprets, creating a principal--agent failure: outputs can appear compliant without being compliant. Existing evaluation measures task accuracy but not whether governance constrains behaviour at the decision rationale level -- where regulated decisions must be auditable. We introduce five governance metrics that quantify policy compliance at the rationale level and apply them in a synthetic banking domain to compare text-only governance against mechanical enforcement: four primitives operating outside the model's interpretive loop. Under text-only governance, 27% of deferrals carry no decision-relevant information. Mechanical enforcement reduces this rate by 73%, more than doubles deferral information content, and raises task accuracy from MCC~$0.43$ to $0.88$. The improvement is driven by architectural separation: LLM-generated rationales under mechanical enforcement show comparable CDL to text-only governance -- the gain comes from removing clear-cut decisions from the model's control. A causal ablation confirms that each primitive is individually necessary. Our central finding is a governance-task decoupling: under structural stress, text-only governance degrades on both dimensions simultaneously, whereas mechanical enforcement preserves governance quality even as task performance drops. This implies that governance and task evaluation are distinct axes: accuracy is not a sufficient proxy for governance in regulated AI systems.

</details>


### [91] [Video2GUI: Synthesizing Large-Scale Interaction Trajectories for Generalized GUI Agent Pretraining](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14747v1)
*Weimin Xiong,Shuhao Gu,Bowen Ye,Zihao Yue,Lei Li,Feifan Song,Sujian Li,Hao Tian*

Result: 在WildGUI上预训练Qwen2.5-VL和Mimo-VL，在多个GUI定位和动作基准上提升5-20%，匹配或超越SOTA。

中文摘要：多模态大语言模型的最新进展推动了对图形用户界面（GUI）代理的兴趣日益增长，但其泛化能力仍然受到缺乏覆盖多样化真实世界应用的大规模训练数据的制约。现有数据集严重依赖昂贵的人工标注，且通常局限于狭窄领域。为解决这一挑战，我们提出了Video2GUI，一个全自动框架，直接从无标签的互联网视频中提取基于交互轨迹的GUI。Video2GUI采用粗到细的过滤策略来识别高质量的GUI教程视频，并将其转换为结构化代理轨迹。将该流程应用于5亿条视频元数据，我们构建了WildGUI，一个包含1200万条交互轨迹的大型数据集，覆盖超过1500个应用和网站。在WildGUI上预训练Qwen2.5-VL和Mimo-VL，在多个GUI定位和动作基准上取得了5-20%的持续改进，匹配或超越了最先进的性能。我们将发布WildGUI数据集和Video2GUI流程，以支持GUI代理的未来研究。

Original abstract: Recent advances in multimodal large language models have driven growing interest in graphical user interface (GUI) agents, yet their generalization remains constrained by the scarcity of large-scale training data spanning diverse real-world applications. Existing datasets rely heavily on costly manual annotations and are typically confined to narrow domains. To address this challenge, we propose Video2GUI, a fully automated framework that extracts grounded GUI interaction trajectories directly from unlabeled Internet videos. Video2GUI employs a coarse-to-fine filtering strategy to identify high-quality GUI tutorial videos and convert them into structured agent trajectories. Applying this pipeline to 500 million video metadata entries, we construct WildGUI, a large-scale dataset containing 12 million interaction trajectories spanning over 1,500 applications and websites. Pre-training Qwen2.5-VL and Mimo-VL on WildGUI yields consistent improvements of 5-20% across multiple GUI grounding and action benchmarks, matching or surpassing state-of-the-art performance. We will release both the WildGUI dataset and the Video2GUI pipeline to support future research of GUI agents.
